U.S. Senator Borah Strongly Advocates Recognition of Soviet Russia 59

Focuses on Developing Markets

But Labor Circles Declare Opposition

(Washington) U.S. Senator Borah recently spoke at length before the Senate Foreign Relations Committee on the issue of recognizing Soviet Russia, saying that he believed this move would help salvage the world's economic depression, and would be particularly beneficial to the Far Eastern situation. After discussing in detail the issues caused by Japan's Manchurian policy and the establishment of a puppet government, Borah stated that if the United States established diplomatic relations with Soviet Russia, few important world events would remain unaffected. We must pay attention to world peace, disarmament, economic recovery, increased trade, and reduced unemployment. Recognizing Russia is related to all of these. Furthermore, establishing diplomatic relations between the U.S. and Russia would bring many important benefits. First, it would directly benefit the issues of peace and disarmament. Second, it would directly influence the recovery of trade and the economy. Russia is the largest undeveloped market in the world for American goods. Other countries are seizing various opportunities to increase trade with Russia. We often hear of disputes between this country or that country and Soviet Russia, but upon investigation, the resolution of these disputes often involves increased business relations. If the U.S. can sell more goods abroad, we can provide more jobs for our people. I heard a few days ago that a major New York merchant lost a large amount of trade with Russia to Germany, England, and France in the past two years. Now, Soviet Russia and China are the two largest undeveloped markets for American goods. I wonder what we will do when public works construction is completed, roads are all built, and the national treasury is exhausted. If we do not find markets to sell goods, the unemployment problem will remain unresolved. Therefore, we must make every effort to focus on expanding foreign trade. China has 400 million people, and Russia has 150 million people, truly the largest undeveloped markets in the world. Since we can no longer expand markets in Europe, we can only cultivate business relations with Russia to gain a large market in the future. (29th National Telegram)

(Washington) American Federation of Labor President Green stated today that the AFL still opposes formally recognizing Soviet Russia until it publicly abandons "world revolutionaryism." The AFL will adhere to this principle without compromise. He stated that because leaders in American politics and business have recently launched a fierce campaign to recognize Soviet Russia, he is issuing this statement on behalf of the labor community, solely to correct the mistaken impression that labor's attitude has changed. He emphasized that all such rumors are false and that the American labor community firmly upholds this position. Green also mentioned the recent speeches by Senator Borah and Walsh advocating for the recognition of Soviet Russia, stating that while the current situation for American workers is extremely difficult, recognizing Soviet Russia would not help. (29th National Telegram)

Reuters, Berlin, 30th – National Socialist Party leader Hitler has been appointed German Chancellor as a result of a meeting between President Hindenburg, National People's Party leader Hugenberg, National Socialist Party leader Hitler, and former Chancellor Papen. It is reported that Papen stated during the meeting that forming a government based on the principle of a parliamentary majority was impossible. Political circles expect the President to grant Hitler the power to dissolve the Reichstag and arrange new elections. The new members of Hitler's government are expected to be Frick as Minister of Interior, Neurath remaining as Minister of Foreign Affairs, Seldte, the leader of the Stahlhelm, as Minister of Labor, and Hugenberg as Minister of Economics and Agriculture. It is widely believed that Reichstag President Göring will be a minister without portfolio, in charge of Prussian defense affairs, and General Blomberg will be Minister of Defense. Hitler's efforts to form a new cabinet with a Reichstag majority failed due to the opposition of the Centre Party, which demanded that the National Socialist Party leader provide constitutional guarantees to prevent actions exceeding the constitution. Hitler insisted on appointing National Socialists to the most important ministerial positions and advocated formally recognizing the National Socialist Party's Storm Troopers, following the example of the Italian Fascist Party.

Although the cabinet does not have a strong foundation, its members can gain the support of the Stahlhelm and the National Socialist Party's Storm Troopers. Organized labor parties strongly disapprove of this cabinet.

Havas, Berlin, 30th – The formation of Hitler's cabinet has resolved a crucial stage of Germany's internal political crisis. Since the spring of last year, the issue of the National Socialist Party's participation in the government has occupied an important position in domestic politics. Every change of cabinet has triggered the entire issue of the National Socialist movement within the country. The downfall of the previous Brüning, Papen, and Schleicher cabinets was due to the unresolved nature of this issue. The nature of this new cabinet is a right-wing coalition cabinet, formed by the three leaders of the right wing: Hitler, Hugenberg, and Schleicher, united to form a new mixed cabinet. Hitler being appointed Chancellor is a great success for him, and his previous repeated refusal to participate in a cabinet without him as Chancellor has now proven his strategy correct. Due to the pressure from the National People's Party and Hugenberg, Hitler finally relinquished the position of Prussian Administrative Commissioner, but because Göring was appointed acting Minister of Interior of the state of Prussia, Hitler can still maintain his influence in Germany's largest state (Prussia). The organization of the new cabinet was initiated by Papen, thus enhancing Papen's personal position. Since the famous meeting between Hitler and Papen in Cologne, Papen has continued to utilize President Hindenburg's sympathy and trust, concentrating his efforts to promote the downfall of the Schleicher cabinet, while simultaneously organizing a right-wing coalition cabinet to replace it. Although this cabinet has Hitler as Chancellor, the nationalist right-wing parties still possess considerable power. Compared to a cabinet formed solely by Hitler and Papen, this should still be considered a "presidential cabinet," as the new cabinet still lacks a sufficient foundation in the Reichstag. However, it is claimed that Hitler will conduct negotiations with the Centre Party and the People's Party within this year, to at least gain the tolerance of the Catholic parties, as these two parties have a significant influence in the Reichstag. The Centre Party's initial impression of the new cabinet is not very favorable, as the new cabinet did not include the Centre Party platform, but it has not yet issued a final decision. Hitler's cabinet will hold its first cabinet meeting at 5:00 PM today, and the new cabinet members will take their oath to the constitution at 12:00 PM noon.

U.S. Naval Construction Plan 64

Adding One Hundred Warships Within Eleven Years

Requiring an Expenditure of 610 Million U.S. Dollars

Navalists Seeking Passage Through Congress

Reuters, Washington Correspondent – U.S. navalists have now decided to vigorously promote the U.S. naval construction plan, seeking to expand the U.S. naval force within the limits of the London Naval Treaty. It is reported that senior officials of the U.S. Navy Department will seek to pass Lawrence's $610,000,000 eleven-year naval construction plan in the next Congress. This plan was previously proposed in the last Congress but failed to pass. The plan stipulates the addition of 120 warships, including cruisers, destroyers, submarines, and aircraft carriers. Among these, the construction of 18 should begin immediately (requiring a construction cost of $130,000,000). If this new plan can be passed in the next Congress, the 120 warships will be constructed sequentially, and the entire plan can be completed by 1943. Naval authorities claim that, according to the Naval Intelligence Office, based on the current strength of the U.S. Navy, the U.S. Navy can no longer be on equal footing with the British Navy, nor can it maintain a one-third advantage over the Japanese Navy (according to the ratio of the London Naval Treaty). By 1936, the U.S. Navy will drop to third place. Therefore, the U.S. Navy must urgently catch up in construction. Otherwise, when the Naval Treaty expires on December 31, 1936, the tonnage of destroyers available to the U.S. will be only slightly less than one-quarter of that of Britain and one-sixth of that of Japan. At that time, Japan's submarines will be three times as powerful as the U.S.'s, and Britain's submarine tonnage will also be superior to the U.S., exceeding it by 17,000 tons. Although U.S. aircraft carriers are superior to Japan's, they are about 36,000 tons less than Britain's. Only the 8-inch gun cruisers of U.S. warships conform to the tonnage stipulated in the London Naval Conference. According to Lawrence's proposal, what is planned to be built in the next fiscal year will be one aircraft carrier, two light cruisers, one destroyer leader, eight destroyers, and six submarines, to be built within three to four years, costing a total of $130,000,000.

The Fate of the Saito Cabinet in Japan (Japan Communication) 70

The 64th Diet of Japan has officially opened. How the Saito national unity cabinet is managing affairs has been well known to the Japanese people for the past six months. Its lifespan also depends on this Diet session. The most pressing problems facing Japan are its domestic politics, which are in extreme turmoil, in addition to its aggressive military aggression. Since the assassination of Prime Minister Inukai by young army and navy officers on May 15th of last year, Japan, a so-called constitutional state, has entered a state of instability and emergency. At the upper echelons of politics, control is purely in the hands of the old clans; at the very least, it is a joint dictatorship of the Satsuma and Choshu clans and the army and navy. In general society, the unemployed clog the streets, and starvation prevails. Even if the government tries its best to smooth things over, stimulating industrial prosperity with military industries and hoping to restore the market and alleviate unrest, the results are ultimately limited. Thus, the government calls upon the people, saying, "In this time of emergency," we must implement emergency policies. The Saito Makoto cabinet is a cabinet for this emergency. The general ostrich-like capitalists and liberals in Japan believe that the sole mission of the Saito cabinet is to overcome the emergency state and return to normalcy, and that Japan's politics over the past six months have returned to normalcy and can enter the "constitutional norm" of parliamentary politics, with the Seiyukai, which holds 299 seats, emerging to take power. The answer to this question is extremely simple.

First, Japanese politics has not only not returned to "normalcy," but its emergency state is becoming more urgent. The underground leftist movement within the country is particularly thriving. Revolutionary theories have deeply penetrated the general working class and peasant masses, and have even infiltrated various military groups. Everywhere in right-wing groups, there are traces of communism. For example, the firearms used by red secret organizations mostly come from right-wing groups. Figures like Dr. Kinunosuke Otsuka, who are among the best in academia, are now all drawn into the red atmosphere. The sacred judiciary has also recently experienced red cases. Judge Masamichi Ozaki and Chunosuke Sakamoto of the Tokyo District Court have both been communized. This incident shook the entire country and fundamentally undermined Japan's current politics.

Second, the military dictatorship is becoming more blatant. This year's budget has increased by more than 35 million yen. In addition to the 820 million yen budget, the recent deployment of six new divisions has added another 20 million yen. This huge expenditure on military affairs demonstrates Japan's aggressive intentions and intensifies its so-called emergency state.

Third, the economic panic in rural villages is becoming more severe. Although general prices have risen due to the inflationary policy, wages and agricultural income have relatively declined. The so-called measures to address the emergency situation are purely for the relief of the propertied class and have nothing to do with the common people.

Fourth, the use of troops in North China has begun. If China were to resist, and the war were to last for a year or two, Japan would be unable to bear the burden of military expenses and would undergo a transformation. Even if the Japanese army occupies Jehol and eastern Hebei, it would still be necessary to add two to five divisions to the army to defend them. The military expenditure burden would be double what it is now. The temporary excitement of the Japanese military is further prolonging its so-called emergency. With these four factors, the Saito emergency cabinet has become somewhat complacent. The current Diet session cannot but be cautious. The "budget bill" is the greatest hurdle for the Saito cabinet. There are many points that can be criticized and pointed out, providing ample material for debate in the Diet. For example, the measures to address the emergency situation are large but ineffective, and the military expenditure causes suffering for the people and earns international condemnation. However, if the measures to address the emergency situation are reduced, some of the Seiyukai's social base – landlords and usurers – will rise up in opposition, causing an accident in the Seiyukai's fundamental base. Therefore, they dare not have different opinions on the measures to address the emergency situation. The military expenditure is even more powerful than the measures to address the emergency situation. Who dares to challenge the army's anger, which is armed with guns and swords, by raising the banner of protecting the Japanese Empire?

Besides this, there are no "valuable issues" sufficient to challenge the government and win the trust of the Japanese people. Therefore, even if the Seiyukai wants to actively seize power and abandon its self-respecting stance, it is forced by the environment to have no more effective method than self-respect.

In the 64th Diet, if the Seiyukai urgently rises up to overthrow the Saito cabinet, it is not impossible. However, if the power can be handed over to the Seiyukai after the Saito cabinet falls, the Seiyukai will definitely make a desperate attempt to replace Saito. But according to the current political situation in Japan, everything must be controlled by the military. The Seiyukai's hope of forming a cabinet is extremely small. It is feared that the successor after Saito falls will be even more authoritarian than the current Saito, and the political situation will be worse than it is now, or it will be largely controlled by the military, or even completely controlled by the military, or even a purely military cabinet. Therefore, the Seiyukai and the Minseito must be cautious in everything to preserve a glimmer of hope for constitutionalism. Even Takashi Hara, who is old and respected, must still rely on the military's nod of approval. The situation is even worse for others. If the Seiyukai and the Minseito are willing to unite and form a cabinet together, it may still be possible. However, both the Seiyukai and the Minseito are controlled by the zaibatsu and are extremely dissatisfied with most young military officers. The decline of parliamentary politics is an inevitable trend of the times. In addition, Japanese political parties have lost all credibility. Even if they form a cabinet, it would only be a puppet of the military. Moreover, the Seiyukai has an absolute majority of seats, making it difficult for the two parties to continue to cooperate. Therefore, although the Saito cabinet cannot overcome the emergency state and cannot meet the hopes of the capitalists, it still has the possibility of surviving the 64th Diet. The Japanese political situation will inevitably continue to waver, and the military will continue to control it in order to muddle through its national affairs. As for foreign affairs, it will continue to be aggressive. (Sent from Tokyo on January 27th)

Shantou Organizes Public Air Defense Committee 72

Auctioning Confiscated Enemy Goods to Raise Funds

Preparatory Committee Members Already Selected from All Walks of Life

A Shantou communication: Since the establishment of the Anti-Japanese Association, the people of Shantou have registered and sealed up all enemy goods in various shops, prohibiting their sale. For more than a year, this has been very effective, and shops selling enemy goods have gradually closed down. Occasionally, unscrupulous merchants secretly transport cloth, miscellaneous goods, Korean ginseng, alcohol, white sugar, etc., but they are caught and punished by the National Salvation Association, either by sealing the shop and parading the people through the streets, by burning their goods, or by sinking the enemy goods into the sea, in large quantities. Unscrupulous merchants are increasingly frightened. Merchants who generally transport enemy goods have repeatedly created [spaces in original] enemy goods [spaces in original] in the past six months. On the 16th of this month, the Municipal Party Department suddenly received an order from the Provincial Party Department, instructing it to notify the Anti-Japanese Association and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to allow all the soybeans and bean cakes previously sealed up by the Anti-Japanese Association to be unsealed and sold. After this order was issued, all sectors of the city were shocked. About one hundred representatives attended the meeting that day, discussing various proposals and debating fiercely. In the end, they still passed the proposal to unseal all enemy goods in the city, and the proceeds from the auction would be allocated 50% to air defense expenses. In addition, they would borrow two months' rent from the citizens, collected in two installments, borne by the owners. Shops must pay a commercial license tax, calculated at 5% of the capital. There are no statistics on the value of the enemy goods sealed up in Shantou, but it is said to be roughly about one million two hundred thousand yuan. If 50% is allocated, it would be at least five million yuan. On the same day, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Hotel Association, the First Municipal High School, Tongji High School, the Telegraph Workers' Union, the Iron Workers' Union, the Overseas Chinese Mutual Aid Society, the Municipal Education Association, and various National Salvation Associations were elected as members of the public air defense committee. A Beiping communication: Han Deming, the nephew of Han Liru, the former acting chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, came to Beiping with Han's family the day before yesterday. According to Han Deming, the details of Han Liru's escape are as follows:

"Chairman Han (Liru) is my uncle. He previously served as the magistrate of Luobei County. In addition, I escorted the Chairman's family to Beiping. I did not know about the rumors of my uncle's martyrdom when I was in Heilongjiang. It was only after arriving in Beiping that I learned that people in Beiping believed my uncle had died in Heilongjiang long ago. In fact, after Chairman Ma was surrounded by the Japanese army in the battle of Daqingshan, his Chief of Staff Han Shupeng disappeared in Heilongjiang and has not been found since. My uncle's name is Shuye, so when the telegram was sent to the mainland, it was mistaken for my uncle's martyrdom. At that time, my uncle was pursued by the Japanese army and escaped into the mountains. He lived in the mountains for two months, changed into farmer's clothes, and lived with opium-smoking bandits and those who gathered mushrooms and fungus. The suffering was indescribable. Later, he disguised himself as a Taoist priest and left the mountains alone. At that time, there were Japanese soldiers stationed at all the mountain passes, but when they saw my uncle dressed as a Taoist priest, nothing unexpected happened. After escaping, he went to find Chairman Ma, who was in Nehe at the time. When Han was in the mountains, Chairman Ma's subordinates mistakenly believed that my uncle had defected to Ding and Li, so when Ma sent a telegram from Nehe, he said that Chairman Han Liru had absconded with funds and issued an arrest warrant, sealing up all the family's belongings. After escaping from the mountains, he sent Deng Wen to see Chairman Ma to explain the misunderstanding. Therefore, after seeing Ma, he remained Ma's secretary-general. Ma immediately revoked the arrest warrant and returned the sealed property. When Su and Ma failed and entered Russia, my uncle accompanied Su and Ma into Russia. He disguised himself as a soldier in Russia and is now in Moscow. It is said that someone received a telegram stating that Su, Ma, and others have already departed from Russia. My uncle should also return to the country to continue the fight against Japan. This time, sending the family to Beiping was also his idea, as he informed Heihe by telephone when he met Ma in Nehe, and so on."

Feng Sends 10,000 Leather Vests to Anti-Japanese Soldiers 74

Lu Yongxiang Also Donates 6,000 Pairs of Wool Socks

A Beiping communication: Feng Yuxiang is one of the strongest advocates for armed resistance against Japan. Concerned about the soldiers on the front lines, who are defending against a strong enemy in freezing weather, he has personally raised 50,000 yuan from various sources to purchase 10,000 military leather vests, distributing 3,000 to Zhang Xueliang's troops, 2,000 each to Song Zheyuan, Pang Bingxun, and Sun Dianying's troops, and 1,000 to Gao Guizi's troops. Feng also sent a letter to Zhang Xueliang, expressing his condolences. The original text is as follows: "To Brother Hanqing, With the fall of Yu Pass, North China is in danger. The ambition of the violent Japanese is growing. I am deeply comforted to hear that you are planning to defend and support in difficult times. I am living in seclusion on the frontier, with national worries on my mind, and I cannot express my grief and indignation. Recently, I saw in the newspaper that the soldiers on the front lines who are killing the enemy are braving bullets and severe cold, and dying not only in battle but also from the severe wind and snow. This is extremely painful. With a formidable enemy at hand, I cannot share the hardships with the soldiers on the front lines. I am ashamed and remorseful. I have recently raised a small amount of money and rushed to make 10,000 long leather vests, entrusting comrades Deng Zhongzhi and Li Shifu to send 3,000 of them. Please inspect and accept them and distribute them to the soldiers on the front lines for warmth. The remaining 7,000 have been distributed to the troops led by Comrades Meiming, Zhegeng, and Chen Pei Wu. This small contribution is not enough, but if I can raise more funds, I will continue to do so. This is only the utmost of my ability in a desperate situation. Furthermore, the wounded soldiers in this Yu Pass battle are tragic and glorious sacrifices. I cannot personally express my condolences, but I cherish my admiration. I have prepared some gifts to be sent together, and I hope you will pass them on to the brave soldiers. These humble items are a token of my respect. The enemy's ambition is deepening, and national hatred must be avenged. I hope you will take care of yourself for the future. The letter does not express all my thoughts. Respectfully wishing you effort, Feng Yuxiang, the 19th day of the 1st month of the 22nd year."

Lu Yongxiang, the former governor of Zhejiang, has been living in seclusion in Tianjin since he resigned from office, devoted to Buddhism and indifferent to worldly affairs. However, his patriotism is as strong as ever. After the Yu Pass disaster, the He Brigade fought bravely against the enemy, sleeping on their weapons and shedding blood in the freezing weather. Their divine power, loyalty, and bravery are admirable. Seeing that various National Salvation Associations are collecting donations for consolation, and those who contribute are extremely enthusiastic, he generously donated 3,000 yuan and personally purchased 6,000 pairs of high-quality wool socks, specifically designated for the He Brigade. This shows that the Chinese people are extremely united in their resistance against Japan, regardless of their social status. (25th)

Local News

1.4 Million Tons of Australian Wheat Begins Shipping to Shanghai 83

Valued at 70 Million Yuan

Transported by 100 Ships

Australia had an excellent wheat harvest last year. Due to excessive inventory, the country sold it to China at a low price. It is reported that the Australian wheat purchased by various flour mills in China totals 1.38 million tons, valued at 68 million yuan at 50 yuan per ton. The reporter of this newspaper believes that the import of foreign wheat has a significant impact on the diet of our people, so we went to various parties to conduct a thorough investigation and will record the situation as follows:

Purchase Quantity In order to provide relief to the national flood disaster last year, the Ministry of Finance purchased 400,000 tons of American wheat for the construction of the Jianghan-Huaihe levee as a work-for-relief program. Australia had a bumper wheat harvest last year and had excess inventory, so it sold it to China at a low price. Flour mills in China rushed to sign orders, and the total number of transactions reached 1.38 million tons, totaling 23.135 million stones. The quantity is one and a half times more than the American wheat purchased by the national government. At the average low price of 50 yuan per ton, it also requires 68 million yuan, and the actual price is likely to be even higher.

Shipment After the Australian wheat was purchased by various flour mills, it was chartered by Australian cargo owners for shipment. It is reported that both parties have agreed to ship it to Shanghai in one hundred shipments. All shipments are loaded at the port of Sydney, Australia. Australian cargo owners have chartered one hundred British and Nourished Lun ships for shipment. The Shanghai side is responsible for carrying this large quantity of wheat to Shanghai by Tianxiang Shunheng and other companies. The freight per ton is calculated at 13 shillings. The freight alone requires 15 million yuan.

Arrived Wheat The first batch of Australian wheat shipped from Sydney to Shanghai totaled approximately 140,000 tons. Fifteen Nourished Lun ships were dispatched to Shanghai for shipment. According to the reporter's detailed investigation, the following ships have already arrived in Shanghai: ㈠ Dar Yin arrived with 7,778 tons, ㈡ Eng Luo Kannada arrived with 9,109 tons, ㈢ Dar Kelos arrived with 7,384 tons, ㈣ Dar Fanluo arrived with 7,699 tons, ㈤ Xuetini arrived with 113,990 bags, totaling 9,050 tons, ㈥ Eng Luo Panwei arrived with 7,500 tons, ㈦ Gelinweishi arrived with 7,714 tons, the above seven ships totaled 56,234 tons. According to yesterday's telegram, the Basweishi and Aisilehua ships are also carrying more than 15,000 tons of Australian wheat and are scheduled to arrive on February 2nd and February 6th, respectively, all unloaded in Shanghai. It is heard that the United Company is responsible for handling all the handling and unloading of the Australian wheat. The remaining large quantities of wheat are being shipped continuously.

Sino-Japanese Reciprocal Tariff Agreement Approaching Expiration 84

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Advocates Not Continuing

National Goods Association Advocates Negotiating New Treaty

Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce 85

Yesterday, a joint letter from the Shanghai Woolen Fabric Industry, Paper Industry, and Silk Fabric Industry, and other 41 trade associations stated that the Sino-Japanese Tariff Reciprocity Agreement signed in 1930 is about to expire and requested that the government not continue it. They sent a telegram to the Chambers of Commerce in various provinces and cities, unanimously advocating this position. The original telegram stated: "We have already telegraphed the government regarding this matter, advocating that it should not be renewed after the expiration. The subsequent letters from various trade associations point out the advantages and disadvantages from both political and commercial perspectives, and the arguments are very clear. They state that there is no possibility of continuing negotiations until the invaded land is returned. In today's diplomatic situation, the only way to seek containment is to do so. Otherwise, if Japan has already encompassed the land of the three northeastern provinces, and we continue to use the interests of our commerce, there is no such way of serving the country in ancient or modern times, at home or abroad. There are only three months until the expiration date, and we are deeply afraid of missing the opportunity. We are urgently informing you of the situation and hoping that you will unanimously advocate that the government adopt and implement it. We are extremely grateful." Printed by the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce.

China National Goods Maintenance Association 86

Regarding the approaching expiration of the Sino-Japanese Tariff Agreement, they sent a telegram to the National Government, requesting that a new treaty with true reciprocity be negotiated. The original telegram states: "To Chairman Lin of the National Government in the capital, Chairman Jiang of the Military Committee, Acting President Song of the Executive Yuan, Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance, and Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry, We have investigated the Sino-Japanese Tariff Reciprocity Agreement and found that it benefits them greatly and us very little. It provides substantial benefits to them but only nominal benefits to us. It is completely beneficial to them and harmful to us. A major mistake has already been made, and our country is suffering endlessly. Fortunately, the agreement is about to expire. We sincerely request that you resolutely abolish it and negotiate a new treaty with extreme equality and true reciprocity to save our precarious industries and benefit the livelihood of our people. We are extremely eager and expectant." Printed by Wang Jie'an, Wang Hanqiang, and Wang Xingyi, standing committee members of the China National Goods Maintenance Association.

Gu Mengyu Discusses the Restoration of the Two Railways 89

Increase Revenue, Reduce Expenditure, and Solidify the Economies of the Two Railways

The Ministry of Railways is Diligently Studying the Restoration Plan

Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday from Beijing to discuss important matters such as the restoration of the two railways. Yesterday, he went to various places to discuss matters and is scheduled to return to Beijing within two or three days. A reporter from the Central News Agency drove to Mr. Gu's residence yesterday morning to ask about the restoration plan of the two railways. According to his account, it is as follows:

Shanghai-Suzhou to Lay Double Tracks 90

The two railways have suffered huge losses due to poor management in recent years. They were also severely affected by the Shanghai War last year, resulting in even greater losses. If immediate rectification is not carried out, the situation will become unbearable. The Ministry of Railways is diligently studying the restoration plan for the two railways. The most urgent task at present is to consolidate the economies of the two railways. The method is to increase revenue and reduce expenditure simultaneously, so that income increases and expenses decrease, and the economies can be consolidated. Then, the railway restoration can be discussed. For example, ㈠ The locomotives and vehicles of the two railways are all 30 years old and need to be purchased immediately. ㈡ The rails and sleepers of the two railways are also old and need to be replaced immediately. ㈢ Most of the passengers on the two railways are third- and fourth-class passengers, but no attention has been paid to the equipment inside the third- and fourth-class carriages. We will immediately reform this to improve hygiene and comfort for travelers. Regarding the request to reduce third- and fourth-class fares, it cannot be implemented due to its impact on national treasury revenue. ㈣ The Jinghu Railway is crowded with passengers. The Ministry of Railways has decided to add double tracks to the railway to increase the number of services and avoid crowding. We will first lay the section from Shanghai to Suzhou, as the roadbed for adding double tracks has already been built. After the rails and sleepers are purchased, construction can begin within the year. The double tracks of other sections will be delayed due to roadbed issues. The various debts of the two railways are currently being repaid.

Continued Discussions on Land Seizure 91

Due to the construction of new railway stations, the seizure of civilian land has repeatedly been opposed by the villagers of Pengpu Township, who have sent representatives to Beijing to petition. This issue remains unresolved. The matter has now been transferred to the joint handling of the four ministries of the Interior, Military Affairs, Industry, and Railways, as well as the Shanghai Municipal Government. A meeting was held in Beijing at the beginning of the month, but no conclusion was reached. A second meeting will be convened soon to continue discussing solutions, so as to complete the Ministry of Railways' plan as soon as possible, while also taking into account the interests of the villagers. It has not yet been decided whether representatives from Pengpu Township will be invited to attend the second meeting.

Difficulty in Transferring Songhu Railway to Municipal Management 92

Regarding the Shanghai Municipal Government's previous request to transfer the Songhu Railway to municipal management, the Ministry of Railways has carefully considered the matter and deems it impossible. This is because the railway was built with loans from British merchants, which have not yet been fully repaid. Moreover, there are significant outstanding payments for materials purchased over the years, which also remain unsettled. Due to these reasons, it is not possible to transfer the railway to municipal management.

Completion of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway in Four Years 93

In order to facilitate transportation between Guangdong and Hankou, the Ministry of Railways is constructing the Guangdong-Hankou Railway. The section from Guangzhou to Lechang has been largely completed and is expected to be officially opened to traffic in May. The section north of Lechang requires the construction of tunnels through mountainous terrain, which will be time-consuming and costly. Construction is scheduled to begin in mid-February and is expected to be completed in four years.

Wang Jingwei to Return to China Early 94

Mr. Gu also stated that the situation in North China is precarious, and the Central Government has long been determined to resist. Premier Wang Jingwei, concerned about national affairs, has decided to return to China early. Mr. Wang recently sent a telegram to Mr. Gu stating that he will depart for China in two weeks.

Full Text of Li Guojie's Appeal 96

Listing Four Points of Objection

Suzhou Dispatch: Former General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (CMSNC), Li Guojie, was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment by the Shanghai District Court for breach of trust and dereliction of duty for signing a contract in September of last year to mortgage the real estate and wharves of the Shanghai CMSNC to the American China Corporation at an interest rate of nine percent per week, borrowing two million taels of Shanghai silver, and delivering 700,000 taels of silver in advances from former CMSNC Supervisor Chen Fumu. Li Guojie, dissatisfied with the verdict, retained lawyers Zhang Yipeng, Sha Xunyi, and Jiang Yiping to draft an appeal to the High Court in Jiangsu. It is now known that the court hearing is scheduled for February 15. The full text of his appeal is transcribed below:

Criminal Appeal Petition Appellant: Li Guojie. Defense Attorneys: Zhang Yipeng, Sha Xunyi, Jiang Yiping. Submitting this appeal due to dissatisfaction with the sentence imposed by the Shanghai District Court.

Grounds for Appeal: The appellant was prosecuted by the prosecutor for matters related to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. The judgment of the Shanghai District Court, Di Zi No. 872, stated in the main text: "Li Guojie, in conspiracy, violated his duty with the intention of unlawfully harming the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, is sentenced to two years of imprisonment and deprivation of public rights for four years. Furthermore, for the crime of violating his authority as a public official and offering bribes, he is sentenced to two years of imprisonment and deprivation of public rights for three years. The combined sentence is three years of imprisonment and deprivation of public rights for four years. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized will be used to offset the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Chen Fumu's trial is suspended, and the 700,000 taels of silver in bribes are to be confiscated. If it has disappeared, it should be recovered." The appellant is dissatisfied with the entire judgment and has filed an appeal within the specified period. The reasons for dissatisfaction are detailed below:

Question of Responsibility: An Essential Element of Guilt. The appellant was the General Manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. At first glance, this title seems to imply full administrative power, but above the General Manager is the Supervisor, and above the Supervisor is the Ministry of Transportation. The General Manager is under the direction of the Supervisory Office and has no direct authority to the Ministry of Transportation. In short, the Supervisor is responsible to the Ministry of Transportation, and the General Manager is responsible to the Supervisor. All of this is specified in the regulations of the Supervisory Office and the organizational outline of the General Manager. The functions and powers are clearly defined. The original judgment held that the appellant was guilty of breach of trust and dereliction of duty for signing various contracts and delivering an advance of 700,000 taels. However, the contracts were not illegal, and the delivery of funds was not bribery (explained in detail in the next section). Even if the original judgment's distorted interpretation deemed it to be a breach of trust and dereliction of duty, it should only be applied to the Supervisor and not to the appellant. Why? The signing of the loan contracts and lease memorandums were all done under the Supervisor's orders. This was submitted to the court in the first instance. If the court did not believe it, it could have investigated using its authority (the original documents were deposited with the American merchant for verification, as stated in the court hearing). The advance of 700,000 taels was also handled under the Supervisor's verbal instructions. Although there was no formal order, reports indicated that Chen Fumu's telegram had already acknowledged the safekeeping of 700,000 taels, and the prosecutor's office verified that Chen Fumu had deposited the funds in various banks under different names. The original trial also recognized this as true. If it were not for the Supervisor's instructions, how could all the funds have been in his hands? This specific matter is clear and does not require further proof (see Article 295 of the Criminal Procedure Law). To convict someone as an accomplice for carrying out the orders of a superior official and fulfilling the duties of a subordinate official with loyalty is to undermine administrative authority. Articles 34 and 35 of the Criminal Law would be rendered meaningless. The appellant submitted various pieces of evidence in the original trial, and the defense attorney repeatedly stated them in court, but the judgment did not adopt any of them. Moreover, there was no explanation as to why they were not adopted or if there were any opposing pieces of evidence. This is the first reason for dissatisfaction. Secondly,

Establishment of the Loan: Process. After numerous studies and consultations, the appellant overcame numerous difficulties and eliminated hidden dangers. From a subjective standpoint, he believed that it was beneficial and harmless to the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. Now, moving away from subjectivity and observing it with objective intent, to revitalize the business of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, increase its capital, eliminate debt pressures, and avert the danger of bankruptcy, to needlessly borrow such a large sum and be subject to all kinds of restrictions would be foolish or insane. At this time, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was like more than twenty dilapidated ships, passengers and cargo were treated differently, debts amounted to 17 million, turnover had been desperate for a long time, shareholders were consulted and sighed, the government was appealed to, but only offered empty words of reorganization. The appellant, as both a representative of the shareholders and an official appointed by the government, bore a heavy responsibility and could not bear to see it decline. Fortunately, the Vice Minister of Transportation had previously approved, and Chen Fumu, as both the Vice Minister and Supervisor, had also approved. The American China Corporation had a long-standing relationship and showed sincerity. After more than ten written consultations and numerous oral negotiations, a final decision was reached. The original judgment lightly accused the appellant of unauthorized foreign debt. In this situation, could the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company maintain the only shipping industry in our country without borrowing debt? Domestic banks had not been in contact for a long time, so foreign debt had to be borrowed. The Supervisor approved it before it was implemented, so how can it be called unauthorized? This is the second reason for dissatisfaction. Furthermore,

Contents of Various Contracts: (1) Interest and Discount Issues. The original judgment cited the prosecution's claim that the actual amount received from the 20 million tael loan was reduced by more than 3.5 million, and determined that the harm was intentional. However, it did not understand that discounts and interest have an interactive effect. If the interest rate is set at nine percent, the discount is 85%. If the interest rate were 9.84 percent, the discount could be eliminated. If the authorities believed that receiving 85% was not cost-effective, then increasing the interest rate slightly would allow for receiving the full amount (the calculation formula was submitted as evidence in the original trial). Moreover, world finance is interconnected. The Shanghai Municipal Government received public bonds at 80% of the face value. Comparing this example, why is the merit and crime reversed? Since the change to state ownership, fragmented loans, short terms, and many clients have resulted in many restrictions. Recently, the water has dried up and the mountains have run out. Other than using foreign capital, there is no other way to survive. Read the initial letter from the American merchant (the translated version of the letter was submitted as evidence in the original trial). Its requested interest and discounts were already much lower than those specified in the contract. If the harm was intentional, why waste so much ink? (2) Right of First Refusal for Purchase and Sale. This provision is a common condition in both Chinese and foreign loans and was not created solely by the appellant. Its benefits and harms are entirely a matter of fact. Considering the full text of the contract, the repayment methods for both the 10 million tael construction contract and the same amount of the "盋頭合同" contract are detailed and complete. All rental income from newly built houses and leased docks, as well as half of the profits from the dock company's shares, are deposited into the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's account to repay the principal and interest. In total, there will be a surplus rather than a deficit in twenty years. Therefore, the sale of all or part of the assets and various subsidiary conditions that cannot be fulfilled upon maturity will never be realized. The right of first refusal will also never be executed. The original judgment regarded the conditions attached to the contract as a simple contract. It is not thoughtful. (3) Application of Law and Registration of Flag. Although any contract between compatriots does not have a legal application issue, there is still freedom to choose the law of the location and the law of the contract. Moreover, since one party is Chinese and the other is an American merchant, it is necessary to agree in advance. Therefore, there is no superiority or inferiority between using Chinese law and using American law. If it is said that the Chinese China Merchants Steam Navigation Company should not abandon domestic law and not use it, try to find that international private law stipulates that the application of domestic law is not sufficient, it is all foreign law. How can it explain itself? Registering in the United States and flying the American flag are all results of ownership not being transferred before the loan is repaid. Once it is paid off, it will naturally disappear.

Shanghai War Resulted in Factory Losses of Over 400 with 40 Million Yuan 97

| Social Affairs Bureau Scheduled to Announce Next Week |

According to the East China News Agency, after the Shanghai war, all privately-owned factories in the war zone were completely destroyed. The Ministry of Industry, in order to compile statistics, ordered the International Trade Bureau of this city to jointly investigate the losses of all privately-owned factories with the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and the Accountants Association. After several months of work, all work has been completed. Currently, they are dividing and classifying statistics by industry. Yesterday, Mr. Tian Heqing, director of the factory investigation section of the Social Affairs Bureau, spoke in detail about the investigation process and current closing situation. It is recorded below.

Investigation Completed: According to Mr. Tian, after the end of the January 28th Incident last year, the bureau began investigating the losses of various privately-owned factories during the war. The investigation procedures were divided into three types: (1) direct losses, (2) indirect losses, (3) personnel losses. However, because the managers of the factories had not understood the meaning of the investigation in advance, or because there were no responsible persons to respond, the handling was very difficult. After several explanations and investigations, all work has now been completed.

Scheduled Announcement: Although this investigation has been completed, the bureau must classify each form by region, industry, and category in order to obtain a detailed report. Although this work can be completed in a short period of time, the bureau's daily work is very important, so it is not possible to devote oneself to this. Therefore, it must wait until next week before all can be completed and announced.

Slightly Approximate Loss: As for how much was lost in the disaster area this time, the previous reports were inaccurate. According to the results of the bureau's investigation, the total is about more than 400 factories. Among them, the Commercial Press suffered the greatest loss, about more than 10 million yuan. The second is the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, together with other weaving mills and yarn mills, totaling about 40 million yuan. According to the scope of this investigation, it is surrounded Shanghai. The counties of Baoshan and Jiading are not included. If the statistics are combined with the counties, it may be more than 100 million yuan.

It is clear that no further elaboration is necessary. What urgently needs to be explained is whether the above conditions harm the bureau's production and hinder shipping. It was found that Guo Waifeng, a specialist last year, purchased two Norwegian ships, named Hai Xiang and Hai Rui. Before the price was cleared, the Norwegian flag was still flying. The conditions were written in the contract, which is the general practice in the world for buying and selling ships. Also not uniquely created by the appellant. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has failed in business for many years. The reason is solid, and repeated civil wars and fatigue from conscription are also a disease. If it is unfortunate that the unpaid ships will suffer setbacks again, what can be done? With the identification of the flag registry, it is possible to use the original ships as much as possible for government use, and the income from the new ships can be used to support the bureau. It maintains the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company in an unequal position, and it also does its best to serve the government. If there is a war against foreign countries, it is enough to be a barrier to national navigation. It is not only the creditors who can protect their rights. The advantage or disadvantage of the appellant is this. The original judgment did not understand the painstaking effort and tried its best to find fault. This is the third reason for dissatisfaction.

Secondly, the Delivery of 700,000 Taels in Advances. The appellant clearly stated in court that the business company expressed its credit, and the funds were kept by Chen Fumu. These are all true statements, but the original judgment arbitrarily determined that they were all embellishments. However, according to the loan contract, the company paid the funds after the bonds were issued. If it did not express its credit, why would the company prepay? Moreover, Chen Fumu actually deposited the 700,000 taels in banks. If Chen Fumu did not keep it himself, how could the funds be controlled by him alone? Based on the proof of this fact, there is no room for denial. If it is said to be an embellishment, what is the basis for it? The original judgment stated that the appellant's delivery was purely bribery in nature. Bribery has secret elements in addition to the normal items, and the result must be nothing. Now the company pays in the name of advance payments, and the appellant also accepts it in the name of advance payments (there is a receipt as evidence that has been submitted), and the time is 3:00 pm, the location is the office, open acceptance, justified, this is rare in ancient and modern China and foreign countries, if it is regarded as bribery, it is truly rare. If Chen Fumu accepts this money, whether it is properly kept, or there is embezzlement, it is a separate issue, and the cart can be put before the horse. As for what was provided in the interrogation court, such as the term petty fee, these are all the appellant's subsequent speculations about Chen Fumu's psychology. The records are simple, the words and meanings are different, and according to the above explanation, the bribery claim is not even established. According to the provisions of Article 280 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the facts are still the prerequisite, and the vague records cannot be used as a golden rule. The original judgment knew that it was not bribery, but it forcibly attached the nature to it. This is the fourth reason for dissatisfaction.

Furthermore, the crime of breach of trust in Article 366 of the Criminal Law requires illegality. The appellant signed various contracts in accordance with the laws and regulations promulgated by the government. Even if there is actual damage, it does not fundamentally comply with the provisions of the article. If the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is a limited liability company and should obtain the consent of the shareholders' meeting, the rights of the shareholders of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company have long existed in name only, the Company Law has lost its effect, and the manager has no other way than to obey the laws and regulations of the administrative officers. In view of this, the original trial's citation of the crime of breach of trust was inappropriate, and the citation of the crime of dereliction of duty was absolutely based on the heart. The appellant also knows that the government's authority is actually enough to influence the general psychology, but the judiciary is independent, justice must be emphasized one day, urgently request your court to revoke the original judgment and declare innocent, it is really convenient. The document is respectfully submitted to the Jiangsu High Court.

Sanbei Yangtze River Ship "Fengpu" Run aground Twice 100

Recently, the Yangtze River is very shallow, and the six company Yangtze River ships often have delays in schedules and grounding during the journey between Shanghai and Hankou. The Sanbei "Fengpu" ship has run aground twice in four days, and the hull may be damaged. The situation is recorded as follows.

Grounded in Dongliu River: The Yangtze River ship "Fengpu" of Sanbei Company, the last time in Shanghai to Hankou, brought the cargo and passengers from the "Fulong" ship unloaded from Nanjing upstream. It returned to Shanghai on the 22nd of this month. Passengers hoped to spend the New Year in Shanghai. On the 23rd, when it reached Dongliu, a place near Jiujiang, it ran aground due to the sharp decline in river water. The Hankou branch sent several tugboats to the accident site to remove the cargo. After three days, the ship was pulled out.

Encountered Danger at Taiziji: The ship was rescued from Dongliu and had already been delayed for many days. The shipowner set sail downstream. On the 29th at 9:00 pm, the "Fengpu" ran aground again in the shallow water of the Taiziji River near Anqing. It was late at night when the ship ran aground again on the shallow beach of Taiziji. The "Fengpu" ship was deeply mired in the mud, unable to move by itself. The shipowner used it to call for help again.

Qingpu Went to the Rescue: After "Fengpu" issued a second call for help, the "Qingpu" ship of the same bureau, which was parked in Nanjing, learned about it and immediately sailed to assist. When the ship arrived, it was already 11:00 pm at night, and it was difficult to distinguish, so it could not be dragged. Qingdao telegraphed to Shanghai to report, intending to wait for the tide to rise yesterday to rescue. It is generally expected to be pulled out. However, "Fengpu" has been stranded twice, and the bottom of the wheel may be damaged. It is now planned to return to Shanghai for inspection and repair, but the flight has been delayed for six days.

Yuan, the Bandit Leader Who Disrupted the Rear During the January 28th Incident, is Captured 116

Formerly Worked as a Translator for the Japanese-Chinese Cotton Mill

According to Guomin News Agency, Yuan, a native of Jinan, Shandong, aged thirty-nine, who formerly worked as a translator for the Japanese-Chinese Cotton Mill, took the opportunity during the January 28th incident last year, when Japanese troops invaded Shanghai, to gather bandits and set fires, looting, and disrupting the rear in Zhabei. After the war subsided, Yuan feared punishment and fled, remaining at large. The Military Affairs Commission secretly ordered the Songhu Garrison Headquarters to order the Shanghai Public Security Bureau Chief Wen Hongen to have Detective Captain Lu Ying strictly arrest and prosecute Yuan. After receiving the order, Captain Lu ordered detectives Ni Shoutian, Chen Liangfu, Rong Bingchen, Wu Tianxiang, and Sun Shucheng, disguised as civilians, to rush to the Sixth District General Office in Caoyang Road, West Shanghai, and together with District Chief Tan Baoshou, dispatched additional police officers to secretly arrest Yuan at house number three in Hefeng Lane on Bailinan Road at 1:00 PM on the 29th. After Captain Lu interrogated him, he ordered him to be temporarily detained, pending the arrest of the remaining accomplices, and then transferred to the Bureau for further investigation.

Various Circles Decide to Organize a Committee to Comfort Anti-Japanese Soldiers 122

The Shanghai Municipal Party Department, recognizing the arduous battle against the cold being waged by anti-Japanese soldiers at the front, convened a meeting of various organizations at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce conference room at 3:00 PM yesterday to discuss ways to provide comfort. Those in attendance included Zheng Chengqing of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, Li Yongxiang and Zhou Xuexiang of the General Labor Union, and Huang Zhaoxiong of the Municipal Education Association. The meeting was chaired by Lu Jingshi of the Municipal Party Department, with Shao Xubai as the recorder. The chairman began by reporting that the anti-Japanese soldiers in the Northeast, fighting in the freezing cold, were severely lacking in cold-weather clothing. The people in the rear should prepare supplies and send representatives to express their sympathy. The discussion then began. ㈠ Regarding the naming of the organization, it was decided to name it the "Shanghai Various Circles Comfort Anti-Japanese Soldiers Committee." ㈡ Regarding the organizational structure, it was decided that the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the General Labor Union, and the Education Association would each elect one to three representatives to initiate the organization. Persons of high reputation could also be invited to serve as committee members. ㈢ Regarding how to plan the economic aspects of the comfort items, it was decided: (A) To request the Municipal Party Department to instruct the four organizations sponsoring the benefit performance for the relief of Northeast refugees to allocate the remaining funds; (B) To request the Municipal Party Department to instruct the Municipal Education Association to allocate funds; (C) To contact the Northeast Refugee Relief Association and the Women's Association for Relief of Northeast Compatriots for donations. Lu Jingshi and Zheng Chengqing would be responsible for handling these matters. Once funds were raised, a comfort delegation would be organized and dispatched. ㈣ Regarding the location of the committee's office, it was decided to temporarily use the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. ㈤ Regarding the date of the next meeting, it was decided to hold it on February 6th (next Monday). ㈥ Regarding the invitation of prominent figures to serve as committee members, it was decided to invite Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Shi Liangcai, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Mu Ouchu, Wu Kaixian, Lin Kanghou, Qin Runqing, Pan Xulun, Xu Yongzuo, Shen Junru, Chu Huiseng, Wang Yansong, Liu Zhanen, Huang Renzhi, Zhu Xuefan, and Lu Jingshi, among others. ㈦ Regarding sending a telegram of condolence to the anti-Japanese soldiers in the Northeast, it was decided to approve it.

Corpse Sits Stiffly in Front of Empty House 124

- Blood Continuously Flows from Mouth and Nose -

- Photograph Affixed to Business Card -

At around 5:00 AM yesterday, Lin Xingli, a Ningbo native who was responsible for cleaning the alley at Fuyuan Lane, Kangding Road, in West Shanghai, discovered a middle-aged man, about thirty years old, sitting stiffly in front of No. 6, Third Lane. Blood was continuously flowing from his mouth and nose. He was wearing a short wool overcoat, padded jacket and trousers underneath, and velvet shoes. The person in charge of the alley, upon seeing this, remembered that No. 6 had been uninhabited for a long time, realized something was wrong, and rushed out of the alley to report to the nearby patrolmen. They also reported to the Gordon Road Police Station, which dispatched a large number of detectives to the scene. After examining the body, they found a wallet, several business cards with different names, and two passports. One of them was filled in with the name Shao Yuangen and stated that he was a detective in the Taicang County Public Security Bureau. A photograph of the deceased was affixed to the upper corner. After reading the documents, the detectives immediately transported the body to the morgue for examination and took the items to the police station for investigation. They also notified the Taicang County government to inquire about the details and urged the family to come to Shanghai to identify the body. Meanwhile, detectives were dispatched to search for the murderer.

Two Madmen 125

| One Man and One Woman, an Uncommon Coincidence |

Smashing Teacups On the 25th of this month, at around 11:00 AM, a woman went alone to the Da Wan Hotel at No. 20, Mingguo Road, in the French Concession and checked into a room. She was reported to be Yang Dongying, 40 years old, from Ningbo. She was led to Room 18 upstairs by a tea server. Shortly after, the woman had a mental breakdown, cursed incessantly, and smashed several teacups on the floor. The tea server tried to stop her in vain and reported to the Xiaodongmen Police Station, which sent officers to arrest the woman. The officers questioned her about her residence, but she gave irrelevant answers and spoke incoherently. They were instructed to detain her temporarily until relatives could claim her. By the 28th, no family members had been found. The police chief ordered her to be sent to the Xinpu Yutang Mental Asylum in Nanshi for care and treatment. The woman had short hair, combed back, and was wearing a dark blue satin cotton-padded jacket and trousers, with a fake wool vest and black socks and gray velvet shoes. If any relatives are found, they can contact the French Concession General Police Station or Xinpu Yutang to claim her.

Tearing Up Banknotes Wu Hougui, a Ningbo native, 44 years old, used to be a boatman. He lived at No. 5, Huaixianfang, Fujia Street, in the city. In the spring of last year, Wu suffered a major shock, which led to mental illness. He cried and laughed unpredictably every day. Sometimes he danced and sang loudly at home, or he frowned and sat silently in a corner. He often secretly tore banknotes into small pieces and threw them into the sky, making them fly like butterflies. Then he laughed wildly at the sky. Sometimes he rubbed silver dollars on the ground until they were half-worn, treating money as waste. Yesterday morning, at around 10:00 AM, Wu started an argument with his wife, Yang, for no reason and beat her severely. Zhou Songyang, the local patrol officer, heard the commotion and came to separate them. When he asked for the reason, Wu, without any consideration, grabbed Zhou's left hand and bit his index finger hard, causing it to bleed. The officer took Wu to the First District, Second Precinct Police Station. During the preliminary interrogation by the station chief, Wu Hougui's answers were also irrelevant. Since he was considered insane, his actions were excusable, and he was handed back to his wife, Yang, to be sent to the hospital for proper treatment.

First District, Second Precinct Police Station Uncovers Gambling Den 126

Xu Chenghuang, the chief of the First District police precinct in the Nanshi Chinese Concession Public Security Bureau, received a tip the night before, saying that a private gambling den had been discovered behind the Flour Exchange on Xinkai River within the precinct's jurisdiction. Chief Xu, after receiving the report, personally led many officers to the address that night and arrested four people on the spot, confiscating gambling tools such as dominoes and gambling funds. Many others had fled through the windows upon hearing the news. The suspects were all taken to the precinct, and after a preliminary interrogation, all confessed to gambling. Yesterday, a document was submitted to the judicial section for punishment.

Major Fire at Gu Tiansheng Cotton Mill on Xinzha Road 130

Sparks from Engine Ignite Cotton

Frozen Water Pipes Impede Firefighting

Losses Estimated at Over 100,000 Yuan

At 7:30 AM yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out at the Gu Tiansheng Cotton Mill, located at the southern end of Xinzha Bridge on North Chengdu Road, Xinzha Road, due to a cotton fire. The Central, Xinzha, and Zhabei fire brigades worked hard to extinguish the fire, which was finally put out at noon. The losses were significant. The details are as follows:

Sparks Erupt from Engine 131

The Gu Tiansheng Cotton Mill specializes in the production and sale of silk waste and cotton heads after mechanical processing. It was newly established by Gu Tiansheng, a local resident. The factory is located inside No. 40, Lane 1086, North Chengdu Road, south of Xinzha Bridge. It is a self-built three-story cement building with more than 170 male and female workers. The manager is named Chen Taisheng. The factory had stopped work on December 23rd of the lunar calendar and only started work yesterday. Therefore, the workers entered the factory one after another at around 7:00 AM. The workers in charge of the machinery and bleaching immediately started the machines. Unexpectedly, after only a few rotations, sparks erupted from the engine and landed on the bleached cotton, immediately igniting it.

Water Freezes, Fire Spreads 132

According to the factory workers, sparks often erupted from the engine when they put the bleached cotton into the machine. The cotton would catch fire immediately because bleaching requires the use of sulfur, which is easily flammable. Therefore, the factory had installed water pipes next to each machine. In the event of a fire, the water could be used to extinguish it. However, when the fire broke out yesterday, the inside of the water pipes had frozen, and no water came out. Therefore, within a few minutes, the fire spread to the entire machine room. All the workers gathered in the room, and seeing that the fire was uncontrollable, they climbed onto the roof and shouted for help. At the same time, the factory and nearby factories telegraphed the fire brigades to report the alarm.

Saving People and Fighting the Fire 133

The Zhabei fire brigades arrived first and saw that the fire was spreading rapidly and that the workers were still on the roof, in imminent danger. They quickly used ladders to rescue the workers first. At the same time, the Central and Xinzha fire brigades of the Public Concession also heard the news and drove to the scene to help extinguish the fire. In total, more than forty water pipes were aimed at the factory to spray water. However, due to the cold weather, the supply of tap water was scarce and almost insufficient. At the same time, the factory walls were high, making it difficult to extinguish the fire. The firefighters burned wood next to the water pipes to melt the ice in the pipes and raised ladders to spray water from above. Soon, the fireboat of the Water Police Station also arrived and began to pump water from the Suzhou River to supply the fire engines. The water pressure of the fire engines increased, and the fire was slightly reduced. It was not completely extinguished until around 11:00 AM at noon. The entire factory was destroyed.

Losses Estimated at Over 100,000 134

After the fire was extinguished, an investigation was conducted into the losses of the factory. It is understood that there were nine cotton ginning machines in the factory, each worth more than 4,000 yuan. There was also a motor, worth about 40,000 yuan, and a pile of cotton silk waste, worth about 30,000 yuan. The total loss was estimated at over 100,000 yuan. A large amount of gasoline was stored inside the factory, but fortunately, it was rescued by the firefighters before it was burned, otherwise the consequences would have been even more unimaginable. At the same time, the Yikang Warehouse on the left side of the factory and the warehouse of the China Merchants' Gauze Exchange on the right side were not affected, which can be said to be a great stroke of luck. It is also understood that the factory only had 40,000 yuan of fire insurance.

Airmail Postage Increase 135

- Effective Tomorrow -

Mr. Dai Enji, the general manager of China National Aviation Corporation, was summoned to Beijing by Minister of Communications Zhu Jiahua to discuss important matters. He has now completed his work and returned to Shanghai yesterday morning. The Shanghai-Beiping air route of the company has been operating on schedule recently due to improved weather conditions. The issue of passenger transport will be implemented from tomorrow. The increase in airmail postage will also be implemented at the same time, with an increase of ten cents per air zone (originally set at one and a half cents). The postal authorities and offices at each station have been notified. In addition, the company's board of directors will be held in February to discuss important issues such as the Shanghai-Guangdong route.

Chinese and Foreign River Steamers Compete to Transport Hunan Rice to Shanghai 136

~ Transporting Two Million Stones of Rice to Shanghai ~

~ Loading to Begin on February 1 ~

Last year's autumn harvest in Hunan was very abundant, and there was a large stock of rice in various places. At that time, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Hunan Provincial Government agreed to transport two million stones of Hunan rice to Shanghai for sale. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company also assigned the Jiangda and Jiangjing ships to transport the rice to Changsha. Unexpectedly, the Hunan Provincial authorities required the payment of export passport fees and other taxes for each stone, resulting in excessive costs. At that time, only 700 bags were transported to Shanghai before loading was stopped, and Hunan rice has not been able to leave the province since. Until the beginning of this month, the Hunan Construction Department learned that Jiangxi and Anhui provinces were exempting rice taxes and exporting rice in large quantities. Two special commissioners were sent, one to Shanghai and one to Guangzhou, to negotiate transportation and sales matters. Wang Qunhui, the representative in Shanghai, negotiated with various local steamship companies on ways to reduce freight rates, temporarily using silver as foreign currency to collect freight. The Hunan government also agreed to waive taxes. Taking advantage of the high rice prices in Shanghai, they plan to load two million stones of rice to Shanghai. Various Chinese shipping companies have expressed their sympathy and have agreed to send ships to Hunan to start loading on February 1. Foreign river steamers, upon hearing the news, have also dispatched ships to Changsha to compete to transport rice to Shanghai. It is reported that the first batch of Hunan rice may arrive here this week.

Telephone Numbers to Replace Addresses of Telegram Recipients 137

| To Be Implemented Tomorrow |

In order to facilitate senders and save costs, the Telegraph Bureau drafted a plan to replace the addresses of telegram recipients with telephone numbers and submitted it to the Ministry of Communications for approval. It has now been decided to implement it from tomorrow. Other ports will also implement it at the same time. However, senders must remember the recipient's telephone number, and it should also be indicated whether the recipient's telephone is in the Concession or the Chinese area. If it is in the Concession, the recipient's Concession number should be indicated to avoid errors by the delivery person.

New-Style Ferry Completed by the Public Works Department 138

The number of citizens traveling back and forth between the east and west banks of the Huangpu River is estimated to be over 150,000 per month, according to statistics from three years ago. However, the privately-run ferries are poorly equipped, and crossing the river takes at least fifteen minutes and up to twenty minutes to half an hour. Moreover, the ships are old and often cause accidents, which is not uncommon. In order to develop the Pudong area and facilitate public transportation, the municipal government ordered the Public Works Department to establish cross-river ferries at key locations. Since its opening, the citizens have found it convenient. Taking the Dongmen Road-Lujiazui line as an example, nearly 10,000 people travel back and forth each month. Now, further improvements have been sought, and two new-style ferries that travel in both directions have been ordered and completed. On the 25th of this month, the municipal government appointed Secretary Zhang Tingrong, together with Tan Boying, the chief of the Ferry General Management Office of the Public Works Department, to inspect and accept the ferries. The ferries are 63 feet long, 15 feet wide, with a draft of 4.5 feet, 75 horsepower, and an average speed of 8 knots. They can carry two large cars. Because the ferries travel

Remaining Silent, the Yu Long Ship Disappeared, No News to Date 139

Family Members of Crew Extremely Anxious

Various Parties Speculate Ill Omens Are Likely

|| Manager Helplessly Travels to Qingpu to Seek Divine Intervention ||

The Yu Long ship, belonging to the Tongyu Shipping Company, which disappeared on December 8 last year after loading coal in Hongji and sailing to Shanghai, has been gone for two months. After customs offices in various locations sent telegrams to inquire, there is still no news. Various parties predict that it may have sunk. Details are as follows:

No News The Yu Long ship loaded 2,400 tons of coal in Hongji on December 8 and sailed to Shanghai, suddenly disappearing. After the company telegraphed the Hong Kong radio station to relay the call without a response, the Ying Ping Feng Xiang ships of Hong Kong Yanzhou Island passed by on the 3rd of this month and discovered the Yu Long's bizarre radio signal. The company then telegraphed customs offices in Hongji, Hainan, Hong Kong, Shantou, and other places to investigate on their behalf. Now, the customs offices in various places have replied that telegrams have been sent to inquire, but there is still no news.

Ill Omens Are Likely The entire crew of the Yu Long ship consisted of about 40 people. After the families of the crew received the news of the ship's disappearance, they all went to the company to inquire about the truth and request relief. Manager Chen Yisheng first issued one month's salary to the families of the crew to comfort them. Now, the families have not received any news to date. According to various predictions, ill omens are likely. They have been going to the company to inquire for days. The reporter met with the families of the crew yesterday, and they all wept bitterly when they talked about the ship's disappearance. Their situation was very tragic.

Various Predictions The reporter from Xinsheng News Agency spoke with the company's accountant, who said that the disappearance of the Yu Long ship was a rare occurrence in the shipping industry. The company sent telegrams to various places to investigate, but there was no news. On December 8, three ships from the Sanbei Company, the Taishan ship, the French ship, and a Japanese ship, set sail at the same time from Hongji, but none of them saw the Yu Long ship's trail. It is predicted that it was either robbed or sunk in a hurricane. It is said that the manager has already gone to Qingpu to seek divine intervention. However, according to the reporter's inquiry in the shipping industry, the ship has not been found to date. It is believed that it encountered a hurricane and crashed after sailing from Hongji and before passing Hainan Island.

Sailing, eliminating the trouble of turning around. Therefore, the ferry can cross the river once in just two minutes. The sailing is not only not shallow, but also stable, fast, and comfortable, which is an innovation in our country. It is reported that the Public Works Department is planning to build a wharf on the opposite bank of the river and another ferry in order to prepare for the convenience of crossing the river. The pace will be accelerated, and after it is launched in the future, the convenience of traffic on both sides of the river will be no different from sailing.
