Based on the previous situation, it is appropriate to consult your Ministry for review and approval.

Total Shanghai Population Exceeds 3.24 Million 141

An Increase of Over 170,000 Compared to Three Months Ago

Over 26,700 Japanese Residents in Shanghai

The total population of Shanghai has been fluctuating since the January 28th Incident of last year due to the situation, with no definite number. Yesterday, according to an investigation by the Huadong News Agency at the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau and the Board of Directors, the total Shanghai population at the end of last year was 3,249,100, of which 3,183,818 were Chinese. The next largest group was the Japanese, with 26,762 people. The US, Germany, and Italy totaled 36,887 people. There were 1,204 Koreans and only 481 Taiwanese. The above population numbers for each country include military, police, and sailors. Overall, the total number has increased by more than 170,000 compared to the survey results in August of last year. The Public Concession has the largest number of residents, followed by the French Concession. The number of residents in the Chinese area is relatively small.

Harming Others Ultimately Harms Oneself 142

Scheme to Slander Devised in Discord with a Friend

Reporting the Sale of Opium Leads to Exposure and Arrest

| Sentenced After Clear Testimony |

Zhang Cimin, a local resident, became acquainted with Hua Gen (transliteration), a Chinese detective at the Xisandoutou station of the British Naval Volunteers, last year while working at the British Naval Volunteers Association. They became close friends. Zhou Fuchu had a dispute with Wang Youzhang, who resided at No. 90, Lane 17, Longmen Road. Zhou harbored resentment and sought to slander Wang, knowing that Wang possessed opium paste and related paraphernalia. Zhou secretly conspired with his friend Wu Xixian. Wu, being friends with Zhang Cimin, enlisted Zhang's help. On the 26th of this month, Zhang telephoned Hua Gen, claiming that Wang Youzhang was secretly trafficking opium from Fuzhou, Hankou, Shantou, and other places to Shanghai for clandestine sale. He claimed Wang was currently selling opium at his residence and urged Hua Gen to assist in a search and seizure, adding that Wang had two thousand dollars in cash in his drawer and that a profitable deal could be made if Wang, fearing arrest, sought release. Hua Gen, a detective from the Xisandoutou station, suspected Zhang was not a good person upon receiving the call. He feigned agreement while secretly reporting to Chief Detective MacDonald. He then contacted Zhang and arranged a meeting at Room 351 of the Dongfang Hotel at 9 PM on the 27th to proceed together. Hua Gen went to the Dongfang Hotel alone and found Zhang Cimin, Xie Jifang, Zhou Fuchu, Wu Xixian, and four others gambling. After introductions, Zhang, Xie, and Zhou accompanied Hua Gen to Longmen Road. Zhang knocked on Wang's door and entered to conduct a search. Unbeknownst to them, the police had already devised a clever plan to trap them. The Chief Detective had telegraphed Detective Hunter of the Xinzha Police Station, instructing detectives Tang Jian and Huierkekaosi to lie in wait at Wang's residence. Upon the arrival of Zhang and his companions, they were immediately arrested. A complete set of opium paraphernalia and a jar of opium were found under Wang's bed and taken to the police station. After questioning, it was revealed that Wu Xixian had instigated the incident. The Chinese and Western detectives then went to Room 351 of the Dongfang Hotel and apprehended Wu, along with suspected accomplices Jiang Liugen, Yang Honggen, Xu Shiying, Xu Yongli, Shen Jichang, Wu Binglin, and a total of ten others. They were taken to the police station and detained separately. Yesterday morning, they were all brought before the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Wang Yaotang, the police lawyer, began by detailing the above circumstances, stating that the police were prosecuting the four defendants, Zhang, Xie, Zhou, and Wu, under Article 370 of the Criminal Law for extortion and fraud. The remaining five defendants, Yang, Xu, Ji, Shen, and Wu, were found to have no connection and should be released. However, Jiang Liugen was suspected of conspiracy with Zhang and the others because he had booked the room at the Dongfang Hotel and should be interrogated. The defendants jointly retained two lawyers, Fan Gang and Du Jimei, to defend them. Hua Gen, the Chinese detective from the Xisandoutou station, then testified to everything. Wang Youzhang also claimed that he only knew Zhou Fuchu among the defendants because he had previously recommended business to him. Zhou had visited his home twice, at 10 AM and 7 PM that day, to inquire. He came again at 9 PM, but Wang was out, so he was unaware. However, the opium paraphernalia that was found belonged to his sister, who had set them up because she was sick. She had passed away on December 19th, and the paraphernalia had been left under the bed. When questioned, Zhang Cimin claimed that Hua Gen had asked him to report any leads on the private sale of opium. He had only reported that Wang Youzhang's family was selling opium and had no intention of extortion. Xie, Zhou, and Wu gave evasive testimonies. The others denied the accusations. After mutual arguments from both parties’ lawyers, Judge Liu Yugui reviewed the evidence and sentenced Zhang, Xie, and Zhou to three months imprisonment each. Wu Xixian was sentenced to five months imprisonment. The other six defendants, including Jiang Liugen, were found not guilty and released. It is said that Zhang and the others expressed dissatisfaction with the verdict and will appeal. The opium paraphernalia was confiscated.

The Shanghai Entertainment Tax to Begin Tomorrow 144

| Still Negotiating with the Concessions |

The Shanghai Municipal Government had planned to implement an entertainment tax for disaster relief early on, but the implementation was delayed because the tax collection methods had not yet been finalized. The Municipal Bureau of Finance recently drafted the methods, which were submitted to the Municipal Government and have now been approved. According to reliable sources, the entertainment tax in the Chinese-controlled areas will be implemented by the various tax collection offices of the Bureau of Finance starting February 1st. As for the French Concession and the International Settlement, negotiations are still underway, but it is expected that they will also be implemented soon. In the future, the tax will likely be levied simultaneously in the concessions. The collection methods are listed below: 1. All cinemas and entertainment venues shall, in accordance with central government orders, collect a disaster relief donation of 10% on their ticket or seat prices. Unless otherwise specified by the central government, these methods shall apply. 2. To avoid practical difficulties and facilitate the procedures for the collection venues, receipts will not be issued. 3. The aforementioned disaster relief donation shall be collected and reported by the cinemas, theaters, and entertainment venues and a disaster relief tax paid stamp shall be affixed to the tickets (if only seat prices are charged and no tickets are issued, the donation shall be calculated based on the actual seat price). 4. The disaster relief donations collected by the cinemas, theaters, and entertainment venues shall be settled daily and reported on a weekly basis, along with the donation funds, to the various tax collection offices of the Bureau for verification and collection. The weekly report form will be determined separately. 5. The various tax collection offices shall submit the aforementioned donation funds to the Bureau on the same day for forwarding to the Central Bank for disbursement. 6. The various tax collection offices shall compile a summary table of the weekly donations from the cinemas, theaters, and entertainment venues and submit it to the Bureau for review. 7. If the number of donations reported by cinemas, theaters, and entertainment venues does not match their business income, the main ledgers of the venues may be inspected. If concealment or underpayment is discovered, it shall be reported and dealt with according to law. 8. These methods may be revised at any time if there are any omissions. 9. These methods shall be implemented after being approved by the Municipal Government.

Arts and Entertainment 147

The Glory After the Completion of "The Isolated Army": Zhang Peilan, Shi Yu, Zhou Shixun, and others of the Dazhong Film Company, recognizing the critical state of the nation, pooled resources to produce the film "The Isolated Army," written by Zhou Shixun, which extols loyalty, courage, filial piety, and righteousness. They invited Chen Tianjun, a renowned figure in the film industry, to direct the film and hired Li Li, Ye Juanjuan, Min Dezhang, and other stars to perform. In order to portray the war situation realistically, they obtained the consent of the military and political authorities in advance, and the Ministry designated anti-Japanese soldiers from the 87th Division stationed in Soviet Russia to participate in the performance, marking the first instance of military-civilian cooperation in the domestic film industry. Unfortunately, on the first day of filming, a soldier accidentally fired a live round, killing soldier Ye Dajing and actress Yang Liuqing. Negotiations with Yang's father have been concluded through the efforts of lawyer Chen Wencan and Shi Yu. The film "The Isolated Army" has now been completed. The film depicts the anti-Japanese efforts of soldiers on the battlefield and the story of a young man joining the army and leaving his family. It is exceptionally stimulating and profound. Film distributors have been contacting the company manager to purchase the screening rights. Theaters in various regions have sent letters inquiring about the screening dates. It is also said that the film has received inscriptions of praise and encouragement from Sun Ke, Ma Chaojun, Zhang Huichang, and other dignitaries. Once the editing and printing are completed, it will be sent to the capital for a trial screening and submitted for review. The dignitaries in Beijing are eager to see the film, and it is expected to receive praise and awards from other dignitaries as well.

Reader's Advice

Youth Marriage Problems 153

| Letter from Wang Chuhou

I studied at a higher primary school for three years and have always been keen to study science carefully. A female classmate and I were in agreement with each other, and we became engaged. I intended to go to middle school after graduation to complete my studies, and then officially marry her. Unexpectedly, after graduating last year, my father called me to go out and be an apprentice. Before I went into the shop, I always thought I could learn something while working, but the day after entering the shop, the boss actually announced my servant work! Up to now, I am still busy with servant work. Needless to say, I am falling behind in my studies day by day! As for marriage, it is related to lifelong happiness, but parents only need to complete the marriage for their children to fulfill their parents' responsibility. So my father has arranged a village woman for me, who does not know a single word, and only knows how to cook and wash clothes every day! Now I have no joy in life, may I ask how to solve it?

Answer: I have read your letter. Your problem is not a big deal. Since you and a female classmate are in agreement with each other and have an engagement, then you should keep it and not change it. As for the village woman your parents have arranged for you, you should write a letter to them explaining that marriage must be independent, and resolutely reject their "meddling." This is one. However, there is one thing. You think your female classmate is naturally much better than "a village woman who does not know a single word, and only knows how to cook and wash clothes," but this also depends on how you see it. In our experience, the so-called female students in the city certainly know how to read, and even write letters, and say a few nice words like "equality" and "freedom." However, apart from these abilities, all they have left is to run around in the "modern" dress of modern girls all day long. Although they are dressed up in a flamboyant and ethereal manner, or if not, they want to go to the cinema here today and go dancing there tomorrow. Today they see someone else's coat is good, and they want you to buy it, and tomorrow they see someone else's leather bag is good, and they want you to get it. Then you will be overwhelmed and exhausted. If you don't agree, then she will gradually reduce her love, and if someone richer than you can meet her needs, then she will "switch to another lute." As a result, you may only end up with nothing, and it is better than "the village woman who cooks and washes clothes." We are just talking about general experience, for your reference, of course your female friend is not such a woman, so we cannot generalize. This is two. Since you are keen to study science carefully, you must steal time from your busy schedule to study. As long as you don't let go every day, and don't let go at any time, there will always be opportunities for you to study, even if it is a very short time, such as an hour, or even three or two minutes. Ask the boss in the name of your colleagues to give you this little time to read newspapers. I think it can be done. This is three.

Educational Progress in Fujian Province 155

〓Restoring the Original Education Budget of 120,000〓

〓Universities Coordinate and Collaborate〓

The original education budget for Fujian Province was 120,000, which was allocated from salt tax revenue and had been in place for a long time. Due to various reasons last year, only 100,000 was paid. Although various economizing measures were taken, the actual amount needed was still more than 109,000, with the difference to be covered by the provincial treasury. However, the situation this year is completely different. The counties in southern Fujian have fallen into the red disaster, and local education has gone bankrupt. Although the 19th Route Army has gradually recovered them, the subsequent construction of school buildings, training of teachers, and replenishment of equipment all require funds. Other primary and secondary schools in various counties are also facing difficulties due to the impact of the local economic downturn and have requested subsidies. Furthermore, many planned projects are waiting for funds to proceed. It is heard that the new Director of Education, Zheng Zhenwen, immediately proposed to the provincial government to strive to restore the original budget of 120,000 to cope with the situation and request the Auditing Office to allocate the funds accordingly. However, Liu Shumei, the manager of the Auditing Office, is still delaying.

Also, Fujian Director of Education Zheng Zhenwen is striving to rectify school education and has been visiting various schools under his jurisdiction for inspection and guidance for several days, sparing no effort. Recently, in order to seek cooperation among the province's private universities, he specially convened a discussion meeting at the Department on the afternoon of the 13th of this month, inviting Xiamen University President Lin Wenqing, Secretary Zhan Rujia, Fujian College President He Gonggan, Dean of Academics Ruan Xiang, Secretary Guo Mengsong, Union College President Lin Jingrun, Dean of Academics Chen Xi'en, and Department Secretary Wei Xianzhang, Section Chief Tang Shouqian, Inspector Wen Yunong, and Chen Kezhong, an inspector dispatched by the Ministry, to attend. After mutual discussion among the college presidents, it was decided to connect the current universities so that they can become a comprehensive university in the near future, cooperating with each other, assisting each other, and avoiding duplication of departments and systems while developing their unique spirits so that they can each become a complete university in the future. For example, Fujian College has recently added a library where many ancient books are stored by various parties, which is enough to provide for the application of Union College's liberal arts. Union College's original natural science equipment is enough to assist Fujian College in planning for the establishment of an agricultural science department. Xiamen University focuses on the study of aquatic organisms, while Union College focuses on the study of terrestrial organisms. As for medical science, engineering science, and mining science, which are essential but not available in the three schools, it was decided that Union and Xiamen would expedite the planning of all specific methods, which will be discussed at the next meeting, the second session of which is scheduled to be held during the spring break. It was also decided that the Department of Education will publish a special issue on higher education in February, classifying and publishing the past management and future plans of each university to serve as a basis for the next meeting.

Zhejiang Department of Education Orders Each County to Establish a Primary School in Every Township 156

At Least One to be Established

The Zhejiang Department of Education issued an order to each county in May regarding the establishment of township primary schools, requiring each county to complete the establishment of township primary schools within twenty-one years. After examining the reports from each county, it was found that many had complied with the order, but some had not yet complied due to special local circumstances or the inability to raise funds. Now that the second semester of this year has begun, the establishment of township primary schools in each county can be prepared and established, and the deadline is extended to the end of the twenty-first year for complete establishment. The provincial party headquarters has sent a letter requesting that the provincial government issue an order to all county governments to achieve the establishment of at least one primary school in each township within a time limit, which was submitted by the fifth provincial representative conference of the province. Yesterday, a separate order was issued to each county government to comply with the order and report.

Local News

Chinese Education Society 160

｜First Annual Meeting Closed Yesterday｜

Election of Directors: Liu Tingfang and Fifteen Others

Board Meeting Held That Evening to Elect Group Leaders

The first annual meeting of the Chinese Education Society continued yesterday. In the morning, chaired by Liu Zhanen, the meeting passed the charter, elected directors, and discussed association affairs. In the afternoon, chaired by Yang Lianggong, the meeting discussed association affairs and issues related to primary education, social education, and normal education. At 5 p.m., Liu Zhanen delivered the closing remarks. Attendees then visited the Zhonghua New Factory and the Commercial Press. At 7 p.m., academic organizations in the city jointly hosted a banquet at the Xin Xin Restaurant. Simultaneously, the first board meeting was held. Details are as follows:

Charter Passed: Chapter One, Name and Purpose: Article One, The association is named the Chinese Education Society; Article Two, The purpose of the association is to study and improve education. Chapter Two, Association Affairs: Article Three, The tasks of the association are as follows: ㈠ Studying educational problems, ㈡ Collecting educational materials, ㈢ Investigating the state of education, ㈣ Promoting educational experiments, ㈤ Contributing educational proposals, ㈥ Publishing educational books and newspapers, ㈦ Promoting educational reform. Chapter Three, Membership: Article Four, Anyone with specialized research in education or contributions to educational work, introduced by two or more members of the association and approved by the board of directors, may become a member upon payment of the annual fee. Article Five, Members pay an admission fee of five yuan upon joining and an annual fee of two yuan each year. Chapter Four, Organization: Article Six, The association establishes a board of directors, composed of fifteen directors elected by the members, to plan the association's activities. The term of office is one year, and directors may be re-elected. Directors of the association are elected at the annual meeting. Members unable to attend may submit nominations in writing, signed and sealed, to the association. Article Seven, The association establishes five standing directors, elected from among the directors, to handle the daily affairs of the association. Article Eight, For the convenience of research work, the association may establish various committees, organized by the board of directors as deemed appropriate. Detailed rules will be established separately. Article Nine, The general headquarters of the association is located in the capital. If there are five or more members in each province or city, a branch may be organized, with a number of people publicly elected to handle the association's affairs in that area. Detailed rules will be established separately. Chapter Five, Meeting Schedule: Article Ten, The association holds an annual conference once a year. The time and location of the conference are determined by the previous annual conference. Chapter Six, Funding: Article Eleven, The association's funding, in addition to membership fees, may be raised at any time when special needs arise. Chapter Seven, Supplementary Provisions: Article Eleven, If there are any unaddressed matters in this charter, they may be proposed by ten or more members and resolved by the annual conference.

Elected Directors: Next, the directors were elected. The elected directors were Liu Tingfang, Zhuang Zexuan, Chang Daozhi, Zheng Xigu, Tai Shuangqiu, Zheng Xiaocang, Meng Xiancheng, Liu Zhanen, Ou Yuanhuai, Wang Diancun, Xu Benzhen, Chen Heqin, Chen Lijiang, Yang Lianggong, Tao Zhihang, and fifteen others. Liu Tingfang, who received the most votes, convened the meeting.

Association Affairs Proposals: ㈠ Proposal to determine the time and location of the next annual meeting: Resolved, to be held during the winter vacation, with the first choice of location being Kaifeng and the second being Nanjing. ㈡ Proposal to determine the location and fund for the association: Resolved, to be handled by the board of directors. ㈢ Proposal to prepare publications: Resolved, to be actively pursued by the board of directors. ㈣ Proposal to request the Academia Sinica to establish an educational research institute: Resolved, to submit a request to the National Government to order the Academia Sinica and directly send a letter to the Academia Sinica to promptly establish an educational research institute. ㈤ Proposal to request the China Education and Culture Foundation Board of Directors to subsidize educational research: Resolved, to be handled by the board of directors. ㈥ Proposal to request the government to stipulate an extremely short deadline for eliminating illiteracy: Resolved, to be handled by the board of directors. The meeting was adjourned due to lack of time and resumed at 2 p.m. after lunch. ㈦ Proposal to designate members of the association to go to the interior to investigate and research the actual situation of education: Resolved, passed, and another committee will be formed to handle it. ㈧ Proposal to request the association to organize an Educational Terminology Review Committee to standardize terminology: Resolved, passed. ㈨ Request that the Education College and the education curriculum be one of the topics for discussion at the next meeting, and that one of the members be designated by the board of directors to conduct preliminary research and prepare a report as a basis for discussion: Resolved, to be handled by the board of directors. ㈩ Proposal to request the association to organize a China Education System Research Committee: Resolved, passed. ㈩㈠ That the association send a telegram to academic organizations around the world to uphold justice and impose severe sanctions on Japan's dispatch of troops to the three northeastern provinces and three customs, and request the government to vigorously resist: Resolved, to be handled by the board of directors.

Educational Issues: After discussing association affairs, the discussion of primary education issues began, explained by Zheng Xiaocang: ㈠ How to promote local educational experiments, division of labor and cooperation, (Resolved) Members engaged in experimental work should submit their opinions for the board of directors to refer to. ㈡ Requesting the Ministry of Education to include various levels of kindergarten education within the school system, (Resolved) To be incorporated into the school system committee for discussion. ㈢ Requesting educational administrators to study methods of increasing educational funding (Resolved) The association will organize a committee to study the increase and guarantee of educational funding and publish the research results in a special publication. ㈣ Requesting teacher training institutions to pay special attention to the development of creativity and the improvement of natural research interests (Resolved) Passed, to be incorporated into the issue of normal education. ㈤ How to improve the efficiency of supervision (Resolved) The association will organize a committee to study it specifically. Next, the issue of social education was discussed, explained by Chen Lijiang: ㈠ Requesting the government to revise the school system and determine the status of social education, to be incorporated into the school system research committee for discussion. ㈡ Requesting the government to actively promote mass education to save the country from danger (Resolved) The association will designate members to study methods of promoting and improving mass education, and then the association will suggest that the government merge it with the elimination of illiteracy. ㈢ Improving and expanding rural education (Resolved) A special committee will be formed to study it. Next, the issue of normal education was discussed, explained by Liao Shicheng: ㈠ Normal education reform (Resolved) A special committee will be formed to study it. ㈡ The issue of higher normal education in China. ㈢ The issue of education colleges, four principles were determined: A. It is necessary to establish normal universities in different regions. B. Education colleges should pay attention to training teachers. C. Education colleges should have full contact with other colleges. D. Secondary school teachers should receive higher teacher training or educational research.

Closing Remarks: After the discussion, Chairman Liu Zhanen delivered the closing remarks, stating that the spirit of the meeting was even more vigorous at the final discussion after three days of meetings, which is rare in other meetings and is very gratifying. The discussions covered a wide range of issues, including high school, primary school, social normal school, and the results are very satisfactory. We are not satisfied with today's discussion, because the Chinese Education Society has only just begun its work. The association does not issue empty declarations, but from what I feel, there are several points: ㈠ The national crisis in our country is deepening, and the way to solve it is to focus on education. ㈡ There is a need for reform in all aspects of education in China. ㈢ Education is a science and should be studied using scientific methods. ㈣ Those engaged in education should be regarded as professionals. At the same time, we announce to the people of the country that educators have united and are aware, and that China, the earliest developed country in culture, can definitely save itself from its final misfortune and will not be despised by backward countries.

Board Meeting: At 5:30 p.m., after visiting the educational supplies exhibition hall of the Commercial Press, a banquet was held at the Xin Xin Restaurant. The first board meeting was held on the spot, chaired by Liu Tingfang. The following important cases were resolved: ㈠ Elected standing directors: Chang Daozhi, Xu Benzhen (Nanjing), Chen Lijiang (Wuxi), Zheng Xiaocang (Hangzhou), and Zheng Xigu (Shanghai). ㈡ Appointed Chang Daozhi as resident director. ㈢ Standing committees were divided into seven groups: higher education, secondary education, primary education, normal education, vocational education, mass education, and educational administration. Each group was headed by a secretary, appointed as follows: A. Higher Education: Liu Zhanen, B. Secondary Education: Liao Shicheng, C. Primary Education: Chen Heqin, D. Normal Education: Chang Daozhi, E. Vocational Education: Jiang Wenyu, F. Mass Education: Chen Lijiang, G. Educational Administration: Yang Lianggong. ㈣ The publication committee was composed of Liu Tingfang, Zheng Xiaocang, Shu Xincheng, He Bingsong, and Du Zuozhou. ㈤ Chang Daozhi served as the secretary of the board of directors, and Xu Benzhen also served as the accountant. The remaining resolutions included raising funds and other important matters.

The Shanghai County Education Bureau held its 275th bureau affairs meeting at 2 p.m. yesterday, attended by Director Shi, Lin Weiwen, Niu Zhiyi, Yang Huiming, Zheng Guozhai, Zheng Shaoyuan, Yan Zhongguang, Wu Jianqing, Shen Jingzhi, etc. Director Shi presided over the meeting, and Pan Shengsan recorded the minutes. The following matters were discussed: ㈠ The request from the Zhuanqiao Agricultural Education Center to establish a native cloth store preparation office attached to the bureau's Shanghai office was approved. ㈡ The Zhuanqiao Agricultural Education Center's proposed itinerant library method was submitted for record, and it was resolved to approve the record. Other cases were omitted. The Shanghai County Agricultural Education Center's itinerant library method is appended below: Article 1: This library is organized by the Shanghai County Zhuanqiao Farmers' Education Center and is named the Shanghai County Zhuanqiao Farmers' Education Center Itinerant Library. Article 2: The center will temporarily set up three itinerant libraries, named First Library, Second Library, and Third Library in order. Article 3: The itinerant library will have one director, concurrently held by the director of the Farmers' Library. Each library will have one administrator, concurrently held by the principal of the farmers' supplementary school or the director of the farmers' tea garden in the itinerant area. Article 4: On the 1st and 15th of each month, the administrator will send the library to the center. After the director compiles and distributes it, it will be handed over to the administrator. Article 5: The itinerant library is not allowed to collect reading fees. Article 6: The center has a gramophone, which the administrator can borrow from the center if needed, but the return date must be agreed upon and the administrator must be responsible for safekeeping. Article 7: At the end of each month and at the end of each semester, the administrator should prepare statistics on the number of readers and report to the director. Article 8: If the books in the itinerant library are lost, the administrator must compensate according to the price. Article 9: The registration books for the location of the library will be printed and distributed by the Civil Museum. Article 10: The director and administrator of the itinerant library will talk once each month when exchanging the library. Article 11: The reading rules of this library will be formulated separately. Article 12: These measures will be implemented after being passed by the center's museum affairs meeting and submitted to the Education Bureau for record.

County Agricultural Education Center Convenes Rural Leaders to Commemorate the Anniversary of the Songhu Battle 165

The Shanghai County Farmers' Education Center, in view of the fact that a year has passed since the Battle of Songhu, and at this time, the situation in North China is becoming increasingly tense, and in retrospect, it is necessary to have a profound commemoration, especially in conjunction with various public groups to convene rural leaders. A large-scale anniversary meeting of the Songhu Battle was held in the farmers' lecture hall yesterday. More than a thousand farmers from all over the country went to participate, and the whole atmosphere was very tragic. After the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, representatives of various groups spoke separately about the situation of the battle at that time and the steps for joint resistance against Japan in the future. The audience was moved by it.

Mellon Middle School Donates to the Northeast 168

Mellon Middle School on Zhaofeng Road, in view of the fact that the anti-Japanese resistance in the Northeast is not only a bloody battle of the volunteer army, but also in urgent need of relief, and the displaced refugees are also displaced and suffering from hunger and cold, and are in need of assistance, raised donations in the school and held a游艺会 (variety show) a month ago. It has now ended. The游艺会 (variety show) raised 265.8 yuan, the teachers and students of the whole school donated 186.2 yuan, and the Consumer Cooperative also donated 6 yuan from the dividend, totaling 458 yuan. It has been sent to the Northeast Refugee Relief Association in the city, which is entrusted to the Bank of China for collection and remittance.

Shanghai North Middle School Expands Reduction and Exemption Quota 172

Shanghai North Middle School on Qiujiang Road was founded in the seventh year of the Republic of China and has been fifteen years since then. Commercial News

Financial Central Opens Spot Trading 185

The Bidding Price Rises and Then Falls

Wavering Around Ten Taels from High to Low

Only Three Taels Better Than Before the Border Closure

Bird's-Eye View of the Whole City 186

During the Spring Festival holiday, there was a sudden drop in overseas silver markets. In four days, the London large bars rose a total of 25, the New York silver price rose a total of 625, the British-American exchange rate rose 675, and the US dollar exchange rate fell by more than one cent. It should have opened sharply higher, but the bank's private telegram only fell by half a cent, giving the gold market a small blow. The morning opening was 793 taels. The market once flourished, reaching 794.5 taels. However, the bank's appetite was not good. The exchange market opened with a near-term British exchange rate of 1 shilling and 8 pence. The US dollar was 28.25 yuan. Although it was tighter than before the border closure, it was not much compared to the decline in the silver market. Although people's hearts did not show a trend of weakening, the exchange market gradually hardened, and it turned downward. First, Huabi sold March US dollars at 3125 and could no longer rise. Later, Huabi sold May half-yuan again. Citibank also stuffed out March, already 375, heading downward. HSBC listed British shrinking 125 and American falling 25. At this time, the gold price had dropped by a little more than four taels, so it didn't matter much. After entering, because the gold was 625 in May, the banks were willing to sell it, and it broke 90 taels. Free Talk

New Year's Eve 227

— Dong Xiaomei

"Once the heart is warmed, seeking my will for twenty-six years!"

I collected these two lines of poetry by Gong Zizhen and wrote them on a photo I just picked up from the photo studio yesterday, because tonight is Lunar New Year's Eve, and after this night, I will be twenty-seven years old!

Indeed, in the past I did get warmth in my heart, but now, only some cold fragrance remains in my memories! Memories may be sentimental, they are always tempting me, sometimes I always think like this.

Childhood innocence is the easiest thing to disappear, and so is the joy of childhood. I was happy when I was five or six years old, but now it's no use just reminiscing, because it's too blurry. People aged one to nine are the happiest, and they know it themselves, but my loving father died that year! What else can I say when I lost the key to paradise at a young age!

What I think I've gotten some joy from is, of course, the few years when I was nearing adulthood, but now looking back, it's only enough to make me regret it, because such joy probably won't exist anymore! Recently I've always been melancholic!

Yesterday, Limin used Wei Huanhua's "Riding a horse and leaning on a slanting bridge, the whole building beckons with red sleeves" to paint a picture for me, I carefully played with it, and couldn't help but feel a sense of sadness, so I tied a stanza of "Stepping on the Sand" to it;

"Red sleeves beckon people, emerald tongues understand, calling for the green horse to stop; turning the reins, leaning on the slanting bridge is a painful loss of soul! The spring scenery remains, but the heart's desire is mistaken, fearing to reach the road; the weeping willows in the building sway, and no one at the top of the building prolongs..."

After writing this stanza, I really only feel lost! Everything in the past is completely illusory like a dream. Yi Han saw Limin's painting and my lyrics, and knew that I was touched by it again, so he also filled in a stanza of "Pearl Curtain" and titled it on the end of the painting for me, his lyrics are like this...

"In March in the south of the Yangtze River, the slanting sun sets, galloping with a saddle, traversing the road back to Zhangtai; the wind is swift, the horse's hooves are light, pulling the embroidered curtains of vermilion doors; suddenly raising his head, the red sleeves are raised, and then holding back, wanting to go back; let's stay, listen to the words in front of the curtain, conveying words for her. Don't say that in the old days, we had a clear tour, a three-life vow, and several times of clouds and rain. The fur coat and horse are tattered in the spring breeze, so drifting! The young master returns, the fragrant intentions cease, and the hair turns white in thousands of strands, thousands of strands, facing the swaying weeping willows, adding to the sadness!"

After reading his lyrics, I thought even more of the joys of the past and the desolation of today, and a sense of sadness kept welling up in my heart! I don't care if my friends see it and scold me for having the air of a "leftover young master" again, or give me other, more unpleasant criticisms, I just stick this painting on the wall.

Tomorrow I will be twenty-seven years old, and the so-called beautiful years, happiness, and warmth in my heart, except in the paintings on the wall, in the dreams of the deep night, and in the vague memories, I can find some shadows, nothing else will be there.

Watching a Fight 228

— He Jiagan

We Chinese people always like to say that we love peace, but in fact, we love to fight, we love to watch other things fight, and we also love to watch ourselves fight.

The most common are cockfights and cricket fights. In the south, there are fights with yellow-headed birds and thrushes, and in the north, there are quail fights. A group of idle people surround and stare, and even gamble on the outcome. In ancient times, there were fish fights, and now magicians can make fleas fight. Reading this year's "Shenbao Monthly" made me realize that Jinhua also has bullfights, but it's different from Spain. In Spain, people fight bulls, but we have bulls fighting bulls.

Let them fight, not getting involved ourselves, just watching.

However, the warlords are not fighting in person either, they are making the soldiers fight, so there are frequent years of war, but the bosses are all fine in the end, suddenly misunderstandings are resolved, suddenly they drink and laugh, suddenly they defend against foreign insults together, suddenly they swear to serve the country, suddenly... Needless to say, suddenly they will inevitably fight again.

But our fighters are different when it comes to foreign enemies. The recent one is "non-resistance", and the distant one is "carrying crossbows to lead the way".

"Non-resistance" is already clearly stated in the words. "Carrying crossbows to lead the way", the method of manufacturing crossbows has long been lost, and must be researched by archaeologists and manufactured before they can be carried and lead the way.

Let's just keep the domestically produced soldiers and the currently purchased weapons and continue fighting ourselves. If we want to do this, naturally, we must sometimes "love peace".

Frontline (2) 229

— Zhu Wen

That night, the three of them were assigned as sentries. Zhou Sanbao was the squad leader, and he himself served as the acting squad leader. Sentries were assigned in pairs, and the first pair was Agen and Dafa. The wind was blowing so hard, whistling and roaring, and it felt a little numb and prickly on the body, and the thick cotton coat couldn't resist the cold. However, the cold couldn't threaten them. Both of them were thinking about something in their hearts. This kind of appearance on the front line made them think that if imperialism could be destroyed in the world, like the cannons and bombs that destroyed many houses nearby, they would feel even more excited.

"Hey, don't you usually specialize in talking about overthrowing imperialism and many oppressed people, Agen?"

Dafa's words startled Agen, who was thinking hard.

"Yes, these things must be overthrown!"

"I always say that fighting is not a good thing. This time, overthrowing imperialism is naturally different, but are the Japanese soldiers also imperialists? I think about it and it doesn't seem to make much sense."

"Imperialism oppressed them and used them, so, in order to overthrow imperialism, we can no longer care about these things. Haven't you heard that when Japanese soldiers see us rushing over here, they run away nine out of ten times?"

"Dong... Pa Da, Pa Da,... Chi..." In the middle of the distant machine gun fire, a cannon suddenly sounded, so clear in the black night even from a distance, stopping Agen's words on the tip of his tongue.

After three or four minutes, another one came in the same way, and the machine gun continued to fire.

"Wow! It's burning so fiercely over there!"

Dafa followed Agen's hand pointing in the vague direction, and a large patch of red light was shining in a corner of the dark sky. Dafa stared blankly for a long time. This was the Japanese soldiers setting fire to the houses of the common people, and it had been burning for several days, and the fire brigade would not rush to put it out.

The wind was getting stronger and stronger. Listening to the distant gunfire, the two of them stopped talking. When it was time to change shifts, they woke Sande and Zhou Sanbao. Sande rubbed his eyes, wrapped his cotton coat tightly, and carefully stepped over his comrades' heads and feet, and walked to the sentry post.

Many chaotic sounds woke them all up from their sleep. Opening their eyes, they understood what was happening. They could only hear more cannon fire and gunfire than last night. The comrades all jumped up from their blankets and hurried to pack their things. The company commander and deputy company commander were also hurrying and surrounded.

The enemy's machine gun bullets flew over like raindrops, and the cannons also flew over their heads with a "chi... chi..." sound. But the machine guns and automatic rifles here also sent back fire without letting up, and the artillery behind them also fired small steel cannons. Their ears were filled with noise all the time, and their hands were also busy loading bullets and turning the gun knobs.

A cannon shell exploded right on the house to the left of the position, and the bricks and tiles flew in all directions like powder, and the ground seemed to shake.

At this time, they had to advance under the fire of both sides, because the fire was too fierce, the company commander ordered everyone to lie down on the ground and crawl, crawling as fast as running. When they approached the front line, everyone raised their bodies a little, and sprayed the rifles and light machine guns like sprinkling water. Just then, the regiment on the right also reached a similar location, and they smoothly rushed forward. The enemy's cannons flew over their heads one after another, and the enemy also rushed forward in skirmish lines. When they saw the troops here, they were a little panicked and stopped advancing, turning their automatic rifles to full automatic and sweeping. The troops here were not blocked by the bullets, but instead fixed bayonets on their rifles and rushed to their faces.

In this way, shooting was useless, and the enemy's bayonets were also fixed.

"Kill! Kill... kill all the Japanese!"

"Down with imperialism!"

This earth-shattering shout covered the shining bayonets, and the people on both sides engaged in hand-to-hand combat. Blood flowed over their uniforms and onto the ground, trampled by countless feet. The people who fell struggled to jump up again.

"Down with all imperialism!"

Shouting like that, desperately stabbing the bayonet towards the enemy. Five-sixths of the enemy had already dropped their guns and slipped away, and only those surrounded in the middle were resisting frantically for the sake of survival.

But the order to retreat came. This order instead aroused louder shouts, tightly surrounding the enemy. When forced to retreat, everyone cursed with a mixture of pleasure and hatred, looking at the bright red bloodstains on their bayonets. (The End)

A Glimpse of the January 28th Battle Exhibition 230

— Zhenfu

In the Confucius Temple in the Nanshi district, after the city government transformed it, a January 28th Battle Exhibition was specially set up inside. There are many tourists. Because I only passed by in a hurry, I can't give a detailed account of these wounds that are so painful to reflect on, so I can only briefly talk about them.

Stepping onto the stone steps, the first thing that catches the eye is the weapon that the violent Japanese used to kill our compatriots. In the middle of the courtyard, a square wooden pavilion is built, and a 600-pound aircraft bomb is suspended in the pavilion. In front of the bomb is a half table, and on the table is the scrap iron from the destroyed Wusong artillery. On the wooden frame on the right is a bursting shell of a field gun, and on the right is a small aircraft bomb. These bombs that have fortunately not exploded are all weapons used by Japanese imperialism to kill our compatriots. What do we really think about them! Behind the bomb are two glass bottles of liquid medicine. The one on the left is immersed in a leg destroyed by a dumdum bullet, and the one on the right is immersed in an arm injured by a bursting shell. The swollen flesh and terrible cracks make us see even more hatred for the enemy's cruelty. But this is only one or two out of thousands. Can we count the actual killings suffered by our compatriots!

In a room directly facing the courtyard, many photos are displayed on both sides...such as the documents of the negotiations between China and Japan before the war, the plundering of businesses after the outbreak of the war, the burning of the Oriental Library, and photos labeled "trampling", "fire", and "atrocities". In addition, there are photos of our army resisting the enemy and photos of military engineering, the People's Volunteer Army and the Women's Ambulance Team, etc., which fully demonstrate our military and civilians' efforts to resist the enemy. Also, after the war stopped, photos were taken of the ruins of broken walls and the relics destroyed by the enemy.

On the left side of the room are many consolation works by Japanese elementary school students, including texts and drawings. What is shown here is the traditional thought of imperialism...loyalty to the emperor, patriotism, military aggression, and triumphant victory.

At the end of these elementary school students' paintings and calligraphy are documents, photos, seals, etc. of Hu Lifu, Chang Yuqing and other people. We see how the enemy's elementary schools are encouraging patriotism, and how the traitors Hu and Chang are so heartless. In contrast, it really makes people sigh!

In a room on the left side of the courtyard, there are also several photos of female volunteers and nurses. Inside the glass case are small portraits of the fallen soldiers and descriptions of the January 28th Incident, as well as abstracts of the report. A Japanese monk's robe and the Red Cross field ambulance bed of the German-Chinese Medical Association are hanging under the wall. The bed cloth is stained with blood, and the startling words are marked on it: "Where is the bone buried? The bloodstains remain!"

When we commemorate the great wounds and strange humiliations of January 28th, we should think...what kind of gifts should we use to repay our enemies? What preparations do we have to wash away our shame? How should we fulfill the unfinished responsibilities of the dead to be worthy of our compatriots who died?

Full-length Creative Writing

The Crossroads of the Times and Love (Continued) 231

— Zhang Ziping

As he spoke, he remembered the scene when Tang Yaoxing took him to meet the famous revolutionary literary master Chen Huamin that night. Chen Huamin had instilled many revolutionary theories into him. He wanted to sell the half-baked revolutionary theories that he had learned to Madame Hezi. But after thinking about it, he felt bored again and held back.

After hurriedly eating dinner at the Ren family's house that night, he rushed to Tang Yaoxing's residence, and then Tang Yaoxing took him to a small cafe where he met four or five modern writers. He had always admired these writers very much. But after meeting them, he felt that they were as ordinary as he was. At that moment, he had a feeling...

"Probably human beings themselves are the most mediocre animals."

He learned many revolutionary theories and literary theories from them, filling his head. But after walking out and being blown by the cold wind, it was like a deflated balloon. What was left was only their sighs, the sighs of this one saying he was poor and that one saying he was trapped.

Thinking of those writers lamenting their suffering, he thought of the emptiness of his own wallet. He felt a kind of inexplicable sadness again.

"Tonight there will be another unexpected expense!"

He wanted to take a breath again, but quickly held back. He walked along with Madame Hezi, feeling as if she had been snatched back from that Japanese guy tonight, and from now on she would be his alone. He felt a kind of deformed and stimulating pleasure again.

"I am completely the lowest kind of animal. Probably this is a unique temperament of the Chinese people. I obviously have "an improper desire for Madame Hezi, which is shameless, but having come out with her, touring around can't be considered a crime. Why am I so afraid of being seen by others, this is cowardly. If I want to have fun, I have to spend money, if I can't bear to spend money, then I shouldn't come out to have fun. But I only care about my wallet, this is stinginess. I don't make progress, I can't make thorough efforts, I just envy the fruits of other people's labor, this is the worst, jealousy... Where am I the noble and promising youth that Liangzhu imagined?

When Haiquan thought of this, he felt that his whole body was stained with foul filth. Besides jumping into the Huangpu River immediately, there was really no way to save himself from the mire of baseness.

Chunqiu (Spring and Autumn)

A Rhyme Pair and a Swing Pair 232

— Zhan Lu

"The north of the house is beautiful and sleeps alone, the west of the stream is like a magpie, this is the legendary rhyme pair. In fact, the second line is indeed in the same rhyme of the eighth level tone of the upper level, but the first line is not in the same rhyme, only because this word "north" is not in the entering tone of "one house", but in "thirteen years". Last year, Wang Jingwei and Zhang Hanqing had disagreements over Tang Yulin's military pay, almost becoming a stalemate; I once jokingly made a rhyme couplet, called... "Wang Zhang discussed Tang's rations, stiff, stiff, stiff..." soliciting the second line, but no one has responded. Recently, I received a letter from Yun Jianyi He, who found a second line in the same rhyme of "one house", called... "Lu Shi rushed to chase the bamboo house, nurturing, nurturing, nurturing." He said... "After reading the Four Heroes of Tang, Zhu, Wen and Zhou, I came up with this second line. Lu Zhu is Lu Zhaorong and Zhu Zhishan. Pushing and chasing the bamboo house means Lu Zhaorong rushed into Zhu's house. Zhu and Zhu are borrowed homophones. Nurturing, nurturing, nurturing is Zhu Zhishan's cry of pain, only because part of his beard was pulled out by Lu Zhaorong." This second line is really an incredible match.

The swing couplet is the meaning of turning back and forth, and one sentence becomes two sentences; the legendary first line is called... "Guests go up to the natural residence, surprisingly guests in heaven;" for a time no one could find the second line. Later, someone replied... "People pass the Great Buddha Temple, the temple Buddha is greater than people." The Great Buddha Temple is only one place in the country; the most famous is the Great Buddha Temple in Ganzhou, which is unusually grand and magnificent. In the main hall, there is a large Buddha statue, lying down, ten feet long; behind it, there are several large Buddha statues. The head of the Great Buddha is pillowed on a lotus flower, and the body is draped in a golden cassock, and the Dharma image is particularly dignified. There is a pagoda behind the temple, built in the Tang Dynasty; the year of the temple stele was the 29th year of the Wanli period of the Ming Dynasty; the shape of the pagoda is square at the bottom, round in the middle, and pointed at the top, and the middle contains dozens of small Buddha statues. There is a small pagoda of the same shape at each of the four corners of the pagoda base.

| Please the Public Differentiate the Taste |

The so-called Northeast is definitely Chinese territory. The word Northeast includes the four provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe. The land there is twice as large as the violent Japanese, and the minerals and forests are so rich that they drool! As for the population, there are more than 30 million people. Now, because the workers and peasants in those areas have been disturbed by the violent Japanese and have no work to do and no land to cultivate; everyone has embraced great ambitions and joined the Volunteer Army one after another, fighting hard to kill the bandits, so that there is a way to survive. But although they are brave and good at fighting, they don't have sharp weapons to resist. All they have are old-fashioned guns and broadswords, but that's enough for them to attack. They also have round heads and square feet, and they are all our compatriots. Although they are fighting to restore those areas, their just purpose is to restore the entire nation! Oh! Drunken and dreaming compatriots, when they are drinking horse urine and eating sand; it is when you are hugging left and right, a glass of grape juice, a serving of tomato mandarin fish! I humbly plead on behalf of the Northeast Volunteer Army, and advise you to save some of the meager funds for your appetite and make a little contribution to the Northeast relief fund!

New Interpretation of the Character "中" (Zhōng - Middle) 234

— Shī Zǐqín

｜One's Own Foundation is Shaken｜

I have not studied philology, and I fundamentally know nothing about the so-called pictographs, ideographs, derivative cognates, phonetic loans, compound ideographs, and self-explanatory characters in philology, let alone bronze inscriptions and oracle bone inscriptions. But I still presumptuously come to interpret this character "中" (Zhōng - Middle), inevitably inviting ridicule from philologists. However, although I am not fortunate enough to be able to study the evolution of characters like playing with antiques in piles of books and oracle bones, the "中" (Zhōng - Middle) that I want to explain now is simply because I feel that the interpretation of this "中" (Zhōng - Middle) has been fundamentally shaken, and I am merely describing what I have seen.

Beginning of Illness 235

— Gēng Bái

Continuous light overcast days accompany my illness,

A sudden joy as the clear light fills the curtain's folds.

From Yuguan last night, urgent military dispatches arrive,

Awakening the poetic soul to turn further east.

Quietly, no one speaks in this deep, solitary building,

Forsaking the week, I embrace the quilt alone.

I love Ding Gong's tearful words,

"A hero lamenting his twilight years feels the weight of gold."

The status of the character "中" (Zhōng - Middle) is probably the most authoritative in our country. The name of the country is China (中國), and the highest centralized authority is called the Central Government (中央).

Xǔ Shèn of the Han Dynasty explained "中" (Zhōng - Middle) as "centering, from ｜." Although the form of this character "中" (Zhōng - Middle) remains unchanged, its interpretation can no longer maintain neutrality. For example, the character "中" (Zhōng - Middle) could previously be interpreted as impartial and unbiased, hence the mediator was called 中人 (zhōng rén - middle person). However, the League of Nations, which now assumes the role of mediator in the Sino-Japanese dispute, is actually biased towards Japan. Hasn't this "中" (Zhōng - Middle) lost its original meaning of impartiality? What is strange is that our country, which advocates moderation (中庸) as its national philosophy, still relies on this paper tiger.

Recently, inferior goods have been dumped on our country's market. Ordinary people, greedy for their cheap prices, all buy and use them. Therefore, those who advocate for national goods are very frustrated. Frustrated, in the Wu dialect, is "甕中" (wèng zhōng - in a jar/urn). (Whether this term is accurate or not still awaits Mr. Zhān Lú's verification.) Alas! In this year of advocating for national goods, if the people do not rise up again and adopt national goods, once our country's economy collapses, not only will the patriots who advocate for national goods be "甕中" (wèng zhōng - trapped in a jar), but all of our citizens will probably be "甕中之𪔀" (wèng zhōng zhī biē - turtles in a jar), and the country will also be "甕内之中國" (wèng nèi zhī zhōng guó - China inside a jar). At that time, regretting and being "甕中" (wèng zhōng - trapped in a jar) will be too late.

We have talked about the character "中" (Zhōng - Middle) in terms of international affairs and the country, and now let's talk about the general public. The majority of our people are illiterate. However, there are probably quite a few who can recognize this character "中" (Zhōng - Middle). Perhaps the carpenter next door or the little brother across the street can recognize it when they see it. If you put three mahjong tiles, "中" (Zhōng - Middle), "發" (fā - fortune), and "白" (bái - white), together, they will definitely not mistake "發財" (fā cái - to get rich) for "中風" (zhōng fēng - to have a stroke).

In conclusion, the new interpretation of the character "中" (Zhōng - Middle) is no longer impartial, but rather collapsing to the east and west. The reason why China is called "中" (Zhōng - Middle) is because it is really useless, has become the target of public criticism, and is a sacrificial victim in the tiger's mouth.

Regarding Donations from Overseas Chinese 236

— Bìng Yú

｜Contrary to the Ideal of the Average Person｜

In this unprecedented national crisis, with the loss of over three million square li of land, overseas Chinese are very concerned and have been actively raising funds to assist the anti-Japanese armies. According to the ideal of the average person, overseas Chinese are always rich, and as long as they are not stingy, they can donate as much as they want without any difficulty. But in reality, how can it be so easy? Don't think that just because you see in the newspapers that overseas Chinese in a certain place donated tens of thousands, or in a certain place donated thousands, you can take it as proof of this ideal. In fact, it is very difficult for overseas Chinese to donate! First, there are indeed many wealthy overseas Chinese, but the donations remitted back to the country come mostly from small merchants and laborers, who are wholeheartedly patriotic, and the majority of the donations remitted back to the country are collected from their hard-earned money. This is the case in the Singapore area of ​​Southeast Asia. Second, it is not easy for overseas Chinese to collect donations, because it is not a few wealthy people quietly taking out money. As soon as someone initiates a donation campaign, it will attract the attention of foreign governments in various places. For example, in the various regions of Southeast Asia, foreign governments mostly do not want to offend Japan, but they can arbitrarily oppress the Chinese. Therefore, in this national crisis, the overseas Chinese's fundraising and boycott of Japanese goods have been severely suppressed. Overseas Chinese have no choice but to change the name, not saying that they are collecting funds to assist the anti-Japanese armies, but saying that they are providing relief to compatriots in the war zones. Otherwise, not only will they not be allowed to raise funds, but even if they have money, they will not be able to remit it out. It is so difficult for overseas Chinese to donate, isn't it contrary to the ideal of the average person! The reason, of course, is that our country is too weak, and the suffering of overseas Chinese is far more than this!

Hometown 237

— Hú Tīwéi

Opium, relieves qi and calms the nerves, the source of life. The hope in Father to make a final attempt became active again. Mother sat on the edge of the bed with tearful eyes, and Hongye and his elder brother knelt far away on the ground. Father struggled once, twice, three times, and finally sighed quietly...

"Alright, since you have this intention, I'll give it a try for the time being."

Father's promise was like obtaining the elixir of the living Buddha Jigong. Everyone was so happy that they walked with energy. Elder brother immediately hired a rickshaw and borrowed the equipment. Mother was so excited that she cut open four watermelons in a row for the servants and children to eat.

The equipment arrived, and Father suddenly changed his mind. He didn't like seeing the dark and dirty gun. He was only willing to load a bit and soak it in Mother's dry tobacco pipe and smoke it. Because he had never smoked dry tobacco before, he coughed violently after taking two puffs. It was only after repeated persuasion that elder brother lit the pipe and he reluctantly took a large puff. In the evening, Hongye was reading a book under the oil lamp, and only heard Father pounding the bed,

"Ai! I can't sleep even more! I know it's a stimulating thing."

The thick smoke from the mosquito repellent made of wood chips filled the room, causing Hongye to shed tears. However, the mosquitoes' eyes were certainly particularly small. They still happily buzzed and sought each other, coming to be close to this old rain that had been a guest in a foreign land for a long time. Father couldn't sleep in bed and complained of feeling suffocated. Hongye hung up the mosquito net for him, sat on the edge of the bed, gently fanning away the mosquitoes, and in the lamplight, looked at Father's haggard face, with his eyes swollen to only a line. He tossed and turned, unable to sleep peacefully. Hongye thought for a long time, and with a smiling face, said,

"Dad, want to hear a joke?"

Father shook his head, "Get me a cigarette."

Hongye lit a cigar, and Father took two puffs. Feeling bitter, he threw away the cigarette and closed his eyes again. The room was silent except for the ticking of the small alarm clock. A large flower had formed on the wick of the oil lamp, emitting only a faint green light. The bean oil on the lamp was also absorbed, leaving only a shallow ring at the bottom. Suddenly, with a thud outside the window, something furry jumped in! Hongye was so frightened that his hair stood on end, and with a soft cry, Father opened his eyes,

"What's that?"

"A tabby cat." (6)

A Social Butterfly is Married 239

— Qiāoqiāo

Mr. Huáng Jǐngwán, everyone knows that he is a social butterfly who shakes the sea; his every move is very quick and agile, purely natural, not adhering to trivialities, and unrestrained. For example, when dealing with you in the summer, he will smile and lean on his waist, holding a straw hat in one hand and spinning it, while bowing hurriedly and running. Sometimes when he is anxious, his eyes will widen suddenly, and at the same time, you will see him shaking his head, waving his hands, and looking angry, as if something terrible has happened. Sometimes when he is sick, he will be like a child, frowning lazily and speaking softly. Friends all think that he is a person with an optimistic outlook on life; in fact, his humorous attitude often contains new creativity.

However, few people know that Mr. Huáng has passed the "thirty" age but does not yet have a lifelong partner; although his girlfriends are like clouds. However, friends, let me tell you! After the January 28th Incident last year, the doctor and Miss Bǎi Jìngrú, a girl from Jinling who resembles a beauty in painting, often rehearsed love scenes in Zhaofeng Garden like a pair of inseparable birds; some friends knew about it and asked him when he was getting engaged, and he always spoke ambiguously, or even vehemently denied it; he released a lot of smoke bombs on the social scene, but very few people knew about this situation!

I thought it was the usual introduction to cultural news, but when I opened it, oh my! It turned out to be his wedding announcement with that Miss Bǎi, who is similar to the tiger painter Zhōngláng. "It is said that when a man is grown, he should marry, and when a woman is grown, she should be wedded. Both of us are grown, so we have decided to marry on January 24, 1933, at the Anle Hotel in the capital.

Amidst the turbulent tides of this era, from the time we get married, we vow to stand on the viewpoint of human love, live a common life, ...... help each other throughout our lives; join the group of young people striving, transform the new world, and reach the true paradise of freedom and equality in life.

We are very ashamed that, in the process of love, we do not have the romantic history of those young ladies and gentlemen!

Perhaps you will not approve of our wedding ceremony, we will not invite witnesses, nor will we make a marriage contract; let people laugh and scold as they please, we will still get married.

Our union is not a trivial matter, but we do not want to make a big fuss and disturb people; now we respectfully express our infinite respect to you, we will not accept gifts, nor will we invite you to drink! Jìngrú and Xīncūn jointly offer."

Friends! Look! Look at this unique new couple appearing on the great stage of life like dragons and tigers!

Shēn Bào Local Supplement

Talk

Selling Official Positions 240

— Kū (Cry)

"My" lord has talked about selling the country. Today I will talk about selling official positions. The issue of selling the country is major, while the issue of selling official positions is minor. Selling the country is an issue for the entire country, while selling official positions is only a local issue. Therefore, selling the country can be discussed, and selling official positions is not impossible to discuss.

In fact, based on the facts, no one in our country has the qualification to sell the country. The so-called seller must have one side giving money and the other side giving goods, with a corresponding price. I ask, has the loss of any land rights in our country earned a corresponding price? We are only giving away the country, letting the country. People are the knives and cutting boards, and we are the fish and meat. We are a country at the mercy of others. Where is there any selling of the country to speak of?

Therefore, I will not talk about selling the country, but rather about selling official positions. "Selling official positions and titles" has always been our country's traditional policy. "The Yin Dynasty followed the rites of the Xia Dynasty." We can know the gains and losses. However, it is a case of azure coming from indigo, but surpassing it. Therefore, although selling official positions is the same, the methods are different. In the past, a certain province sold official positions. The fixed price was 10,000 for a zhīshì (prefect), and 8,000 for a bureau. Now this method has become a thing of the past. Our country has not made progress in other types of politics, but the methods of selling official positions have progressed at a rate of a thousand miles a day.

What are the current methods of selling official positions?

There is the so-called selling the old but not the new. What does it mean to sell the old but not the new? There are endless wonders in it. If one wants to sell an official position, one must consider the difficulties of the receiver. Suppose the receiver is a poor scholar? He does not have much sin-making money to invest. If he has sin-making money, he is afraid that after investing it, there will be no corresponding guarantee and price. So-called "trying to steal a chicken but losing the rice." He doesn't dare to make a hasty move. If one uses the method of selling the old but not the new, then a few county magistrates and bureau chiefs, sirs, already have "mǎikā mǎikā" (money, money) at their sides. They already know the ordinary income and the extra squeezes like the back of their hand. Naturally, it is easy to invest and go to work. This is one of the wonderful uses of selling the old but not the new.

In addition, there is a detailed condition attached. That is, a county vacancy costs 10,000 per year, and 5,000 per half year. If you sell the vacancy, and let you work for a long time, it would be too cheap. Therefore, a time limit is added. Those who pay 5,000 are only allowed to work for half a year, and those who pay 10,000 are only allowed to work for a year. The longer the time, the more the price is extrapolated. This method of selling official positions is considered thorough. It can both gain a reputation for not changing things easily, and it can also occupy the position of dividing the spoils while sitting. How precise and practical is this plan!

Since the official position is bought with a corresponding price, naturally one will do everything possible to desperately squeeze. Afterwards, every detail will be examined, and in the end, it is still the common people who deserve to die. Since the official position is sold with corresponding conditions, even if the official commits crimes and abuses his power, even if the common people want to go to the superiors to cry and complain, naturally it will not be effective. In the end, it is also the common people who deserve to die.
