Common Knowledge

The Reason for Sleep 242

— Yǐ Líng

Natural science in the 20th century can be considered developed, especially the field of physiology, which has truly shown a great momentum in the last century! However, in fact, there are still many physiological phenomena that we are still unclear about. Now, let's just take one of the most common and most important physiological phenomena - the reason for sleep - to discuss...

If a person has a lifespan of sixty years, then he will spend at least twenty years of his life in the land of sleep. Everyone knows the importance of sleep for animals. We can survive more than ten days without food, and three or four days without drink, but we cannot go three days without sleep. However, "What is the reason for sleep?" Few people can answer!

"What is the reason for sleep?" Not only is this question unclear to the average person, but physiologists around the world also have many different opinions, and no one dares to give a definitive answer. The more influential explanations include the brain ischemia theory, the fatigue substance theory, and the hereditary habit theory, and so on. Now, let's discuss them separately.

(A) Brain Ischemia Theory: This school of thought explains sleep as being due to brain ischemia. Why does the blood in the brain decrease for no reason? It is said that it is because the cerebral arteries constrict, and the brain tissue is therefore not getting enough nutrition, so one becomes drowsy. Mr. Mosso used precise instruments to test a person who had lost a large piece of his skull. The results proved that the brain pulse (that is, the pulsation of the blood vessels in the brain) was lower than usual during sleep. Someone also used a very simple, very accurate, and very interesting experiment to prove that the brain is indeed anemic during sleep, that is, they had a person lie straight on a T-shaped seesaw, and at the same time told him to close his eyes and eliminate all thoughts (until he fell asleep), then moved the seesaw to a level position; finally, they woke him up and asked him to calculate a simple math problem (r2Xr5‖?.) At this time, even though he had not moved at all, the balance of the seesaw was broken - the end near the head tilted slightly downward.

Looking at it this way, it seems that the reason for sleep is undoubtedly brain ischemia, and brain ischemia is due to the constriction of the cerebral arteries. But why do these blood vessels constrict for no reason? Some people's sleep time is very fixed. Why do the cerebral blood vessels constrict at the time of sleep, neither earlier nor later? In short, the above two experiments only proved the physiological phenomenon of sleep - the fluid in the brain decreases, but did not explain the reason for sleep.

(B) Fatigue Substance Theory: What is a fatigue substance? - It is a kind of waste produced by the work of body tissues (for example, the contraction and relaxation of the muscles of the lower limbs when walking) - lactic acid and carbon dioxide. Originally, these wastes are carried away by the blood at any time, but if the muscles are exercised excessively and too much waste is produced, the blood cannot completely flush it away, and part of it accumulates in the muscles, so we feel tired. Some physiologists have hypothesized that "we want to sleep because the central nervous system is stimulated by fatigue substances." Someone once injected a liquid extracted from extremely tired muscles into an ordinary animal. Soon, this animal showed signs of fatigue and drowsiness.

But the problem comes... According to the fatigue substance theory, "labor produces lactic acid," and the nerves are stimulated, so one wants to sleep; but newborn babies rarely labor, so their nerves should not be stimulated by lactic acid. In other words, they should sleep very little, but the opposite is true. Newborn babies need to sleep for twenty hours, and after a month, they still need to sleep for fifteen or sixteen hours, and then gradually decrease. In short, age and sleep time are inversely proportional. How can fatigue substance theorists explain this?

(C) Habit Theory: In the era when humans lived in caves and the wilderness, in order to prevent attacks by wild animals, they would hide in caves at night, maintaining absolute silence to avoid being heard by wild animals. Over time, it became a habit of having to sleep at night.

But how do you explain some people who need to sleep during the day? Moreover, this theory deviates from the scope of physiology and is even more difficult to believe!

What is the reason for sleep? - We still don't know!

Yuánbǎo (Ingot) Tea and Asking for Lucky Money 243

— Yǐng Dāi

Although the slogan of abolishing the old calendar has been shouted for many years, the national calendar has not yet been implemented, and the lunar New Year has not been abolished to this day. When it comes to the end of the year in the lunar calendar, the general public will use Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea to ask for lucky money. If you visit relatives or tea houses and taverns at that time, you will have to spend a few cents.

Shanghai is originally a prosperous city. Because it is prosperous, all expenses are more expensive than elsewhere. When it comes to the end of the year in the abolished calendar; if you step into a bathhouse, and this bathhouse is one you usually go to, the waiter will smile and bring you a yellow basket of oranges and a sachet of olives, and in addition to a pot of tea, there will also be a plate of oranges and olives. After bathing, when you are about to leave, if you want to take the oranges and olives with you, you will have to reward them with a five-yuan bill, even if you don't take the oranges and olives, reward

Page 20

them with one yuan for the waiter, one yuan for the back rubbing, and one yuan for the tea. These waiters will still not be happy and give you a dirty look. It is really wrong to spend money to buy anger.

In Shanghai, in addition to bathhouses, the waiters in tea houses also have this set of tricks at the end of the year. If you are a regular tea customer, then at the end of the year, you will also be asked to spend two or three yuan on Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea money. Therefore, those who run around in tea houses, taverns, and bathhouses will have to spend some extra expenses at the end of the year.

Leaving Shanghai, let's talk about our countryside. Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea in tea houses has always existed, but the prices are vastly different from the past. In the past, in rural tea houses, a pot of Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea had a total of ten olives. You only had to give them one or two hundred cash, and four hundred cash was already very generous, but now it costs four or eight cents. In more upscale tea houses, where literati and elegant people frequent, what used to cost a few cents now costs one or two yuan. The value of Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea has also increased with prices.

Speaking from our countryside to the cities, recently, my hometown of Songjiang has also imitated the methods of Shanghai. Originally, Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea had nothing but ten olives, but now it also adds a yellow basket of oranges and a sachet of olives. If you are a regular tea customer, these two gifts will cost you two or three yuan. There is obviously a different color between the city and the countryside.

During the New Year, if you go to the home of relatives, the maids will also send you a bowl of Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea. When you leave, if you are polite, you will have to spend forty cents. If you go there often, you will have to spend one yuan. As for our countryside, it is probably twenty cents, and forty cents is already very generous. In the eyes of the maids, the Shanghai maids think twenty or forty cents is very little, but the rural maids think it is very important. The difference in life results in them having different perspectives on money.

Why can olives be used as Yuánbǎo (Ingots)? Why can olive tea be called Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea? I can never solve this riddle. The general waiters and maids are just using olives as a tool to ask for lucky money. At the end of the year, they use olives to say good words, but they can get an unexpected income. And the general public also regards Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea as a good omen. Eating Yuánbǎo (Ingot) tea can bring wealth and prosperity into the house, so they are also willing to spend a few cents. As for those waiters and maids, I think they are always hoping that every day of the year is the first day of the new year, so that they can get extra money every day.

Record of Ceasing Tears 244

— Dan Sheng

(1) Treasure Hunters

Loring believed that this premonition should not be ignored, as he had dreamed three times of many valuable things hidden in his room.

"You're right, Loring," his wife said. "We should search around."

That night, they spent a lot of time tapping on the walls, looking for hollow spots. Finally, they actually found one. After some hammering and chiseling, with skillful use, Loring found that he had succeeded. After removing several bricks, what was hidden inside was exactly what he had seen in his dreams. Rows of silverware were just waiting for them to move.

How fiercely they stared at his wart-like discovery! But as they were discussing what to do with the proceeds from selling these treasures, the doorbell rang loudly, and the neighbor next door jumped in. "What's the matter with you, breaking through the wall into my dining room's cupboard?" he said, panting.

(2) Rescue

The house was already on fire, and the firefighters were working hard to put it out.

Suddenly, a woman ran up to a firefighter.

"Ah!" she cried, "Save me!" She pointed to the window. The firefighter immediately rushed into the house as fast as he could.

"How many days has it been?" an onlooker asked her.

"Only a month!" the woman replied sadly. "Look at him!"—as the firefighter was coming back—"He didn't get it!"

The firefighter walked over and said,

"I'm sorry, I couldn't find the child."

"Child?" the woman exclaimed. "Who said anything about a child!"

"Then... what is this?"

"This is my foot... my bicycle!" she sobbed. "I've only had it for a month."

(3) Model Youth

An officious old man said to a woman in the train compartment, "Do you have any children?"

"Yes, sir—a son."

"Good fortune! Does he smoke?"

"No, he has never touched a cigarette."

"Even better, madam, smoking is poisonous. Does he like to gamble?"

"He has never gambled."

"Then I must congratulate you. Does he come home late at night?"

"Never. He goes to bed to sleep after dinner."

"He is truly a model youth. How old is he?"

"Seven months so far."

(4) Misunderstanding

There was a great commotion on deck, with sounds of running back and forth, followed by a grating machine noise. The engine seemed to be stopping. A timid passenger hurriedly rushed out of the cabin and bumped into the shipowner.

"What happened?" he asked, gasping.

"Just in case," the shipowner said solemnly.

"The... life preservers, where are they?"

"Those are useless to you now," the shipowner said. "From now on, you have to defend yourself, because we have already done our duty."

He called the timid passenger to the side of the cabin and said,

"Now you see, everyone is taking care of themselves."

The timid man covered his eyes with both hands and trembled.

"No, no," he cried, "Tell me what's going on!"

"We've entered the port," the shipowner said.

Another World 245

— Qun

The wind was blowing hard, and snowflakes were dancing in the air. No people were seen on the muddy path. Three or five rickshaws were quietly parked in front of a row of thatched huts. The scene was extremely desolate. If a poet seeking plum blossoms in the snow were present, he would certainly be able to write a refined and detached poem. However, this kind of scenery strictly belongs to laborers who only know how to earn money to support their families. Counting along the path, the door of the fifth thatched hut was half-open, as if waiting for someone to arrive. Sure enough, a figure came walking at the end of the path. Judging from the slanted posture of his walk, one could tell that he was eager to hurry on his way, but was also careful not to fall due to carelessness.

The figure gradually approached, and it was a small-footed woman, carrying a package of things in her hand. Her tattered cotton clothes were completely covered in snowflakes. She seemed unaware of the cold air of the wind and snow, and just kept her head down, running along the path and rushing into the half-open door.

In the corner of the room was a small bed, where a patient was sleeping, moaning incessantly, seemingly unable to withstand the attack of some kind of pain. The small-footed woman walked up to the bed and gently stroked the patient's forehead with her palm to gauge the patient's temperature. The patient was still moaning and did not notice that there was another person in the room. When the small-footed woman took her hand away from the patient, her pair of bitter eyebrows were deeply furrowed, and she shook her head, revealing a helpless situation; but she still disassembled the package of medicine she had bought after running several miles and placed it in an earthenware pot, lit a coal briquette stove, and slowly simmered it. She moved a broken stool close to the coal stove and casually picked up a man's tattered garment to mend. At this time, she felt cold again, her fingers were already stiff, and she had no choice but to toss the tattered garment aside and repeatedly warm her hands with the rising steam from the medicine pot; but from time to time she ran to the bedside to press the patient's forehead, her face always filled with a bitter expression of astonishment.

She thought that her husband had been sick for seven days. For families like theirs, there would be no food to eat if they didn't work for even one day. Fortunately, the two of them were frugal and still had a few extra dollars, preparing to thank the gods at the end of the year. The first time, they sent him to that charity hospital for treatment. Although the registration fee was only twenty cents, the cost of medicine was more than one yuan. After the second visit, her husband was unable to get out of bed. Every day, she ran several miles, relying on verbal reports to the doctor to prescribe a prescription. After taking the medicine, he still didn't get better. The few dollars they had for thanking the gods at the end of the year were naturally used up. What about life from now on?…

As she thought, the medicinal liquid in the medicine pot overflowed in a burst of anger. She hurriedly strained it into an earthenware bowl and carried it to the bedside.

Clerk Communication

Initiation of the Mutual Aid Correspondence Society 246

Editor: Since you introduced us, we have met several times. It is true that we have become good friends at first sight, and we regret not meeting sooner. Now we have become close friends. Because we each have our own occupations, there are very few opportunities to meet; however, we exchange letters frequently. Questioning, discussing, and researching have been almost uninterrupted. Unknowingly, we have gained a lot of solutions and joy.

As the ancient saying goes, "Studying alone without friends leads to shallowness and ignorance." As young shop assistants, the friends we make throughout the year are often few. Some have disparate social statuses and keep people at a distance, while others have different ideas, and their words are dull. There are really not many who seek to improve each other in learning and morality. Although we two can be called "friends in righteousness," the intelligence of two people is ultimately limited; therefore, the achievement in the future can be imagined to be small. At the same time, thinking of the young shop assistants with correct thinking and rich knowledge, there are certainly not a few who feel the same sigh of "difficulty in finding friends."

After repeated discussions, we plan to initiate the organization of a "Mutual Aid Correspondence Society." The purpose is to connect a group of young people in the industrial and commercial sectors who aspire to progress, to encourage each other in order to improve their own learning and morality; at the same time, to use "collective power" to struggle against the evil society and to seek the liberation of a group of oppressed comrades. We know that shop assistants generally do not have free time, so we avoid time-consuming "meetings" and use correspondence to discuss issues. As for the detailed regulations, the number of members will be decided after mutual discussion when there are more members.

Although our abilities are very limited, we are confident that this motive will not be completely misguided. Editor, please publish this letter publicly in your column as the origin of organizing this organization. Sincerely,

Please give our regards. Chen Ruren (Tian Tai Chang Hang, No. 6 Hong Fu Xing, North Henan Road)

Hong Mingchang (Qun Yi Bookstore, No. 128 Qipan Street)

Editor's note: Since this column repeatedly advocated "Young people should organize groups," several groups such as the "Academic Research Society" have been established; however, the number of people joining has never been very enthusiastic. Examining the reason, it is probably because there is too much time for meetings... Shop assistants are unable to join because of inconvenience in commuting or because of store regulations. Chen and Hong, in view of this, came up with the idea of ​​using correspondence to solve this difficulty, and in the future, there is no doubt that those who join will be enthusiastic. However, in everything in the world, there are advantages and disadvantages; the method of communication can certainly allow general shop assistants who cannot leave the store to have the possibility of joining. However, in the future, when there are more members, the introduction of a question will inevitably require writing many letters, sending them to each member, and asking for opinions, wouldn't this become another difficult problem? Therefore, we believe that a regular publication should be published, with all questions and answers included; on the one hand, it can avoid the procedure of writing many letters, and at the same time, it can allow a group of people to see the conclusions of the answers. I wonder what Chen and Hong think?

Novel

Scholarly Family (Continued 7) 247

— Wang Zhongxian

(4) Out of Sight, Out of Mind

Open your eyes and look... the many women with greasy hair and powdered faces, wearing silk and satin, who come and go on the street. What do they live on? To be frank, they are nothing more than machines for venting lust! Observe them carefully... generally, women with more attractive faces live a relatively better life. Women sitting in cars and wearing diamonds are rarely ugly. Limbs and facial features are women's capital. As long as they are endowed with a moving feature, they can eat inexhaustibly for a lifetime.

Women use their appearance and sexuality to win men's hearts and to gamble for a lifetime of happiness. In their youth, they occasionally conceive and give birth to children because of selling their sexuality. Then, when they are old and can no longer provide an outlet for lust, they can rely on their sons to live. Therefore, women's desire to give birth is always more urgent than that of men. After women pass forty, the ugly appearance of wrinkled skin and white hair gradually emerges. The power to maintain men's love has completely disappeared, and if they have no children under their knees, there is no hope for the future. Life at this point is absolutely boring!

Mrs. Xia had reached this point! She thought that in her youth, she had also spent a sweet life with her husband. Now, seeing him infatuated with a young enchantress, leaving herself aside without paying attention, how could she not be angry? She accumulated depression in her heart day by day, and a gas embryo accumulated in her stomach. As long as the stomach pain occurred, it would affect the gas embryo, which would rise straight up, pressing tightly against her chest, making it difficult to breathe. Life was in between breaths.

When she first became ill, Zhongnan was also very alarmed... Later, it occurred every ten days to half a month. As the saying goes, "There are no filial sons when one is ill for a long time," and it became commonplace. When he received news of her illness, Zhongnan only ordered someone to ask the doctor to give her a pain-relieving anesthetic injection. He excused himself by saying that he had something to do, and he was unwilling to come to her bedside to say even a few perfunctory words of comfort. Therefore, her illness became more and more serious.

Fortunately, she had a close maid named Ali by her side, who often used words to comfort her and advised her, "Rather than looking at their faces outside, it is better to go back to your hometown to enjoy a few years of leisure and gain peace of mind."

Mrs. Xia said, "How could I not know to go back and enjoy happiness? But when people talk about it, those who understand will know that I am being humble, and those who don't understand will say that I am afraid of her. Besides... after I leave, letting her take over as the mistress, I am also not very willing."

"Madam, you can come back after you have recovered at home."

"The more I think about it at home, the angrier I get, and the harder it is for the problem to get better."

"Out of sight, out of mind! It's better to be clear than to stare and get angry every day."

Film Special

Three Soviet Directors (Middle) 248

— Ling He

Pudovkin (Pudovgin B.E.)

Pudovkin was born in 1893 and graduated from Moscow University. In 1914, he was still a painter. He did not begin his film career until 1920.

Pudovkin is more diligent and more engaged in scientific research in the film industry than Eisenstein. He believes in inspiration and also relies on method. Some say that Eisenstein's films are like shouts, while Pudovkin's works are like songs.

Pudovkin often produces a kind of vivid power due to the appropriate selection of the elements of the script, and due to the feeling and concept of human beings. He has a great talent, especially for acting. This can evoke the resonance of the audience and reach the highest peak of expression in "Mother" and "The End of St. Petersburg."

As mentioned earlier, he makes films with a strict scientific spirit. In addition, he has a natural musical intelligence, so a pure emotion often gushes out in his works. He strives to make the film's composition close to musical composition. He fully understands that in film as in music, movement arises from the expression of images. The rhythm that is organized by its movement is generated by the sequence of images and the duration of images. Therefore, he believes that the importance of rhythm lies in making its effect completely opposite to that of ordinary spatial art, and making the audience's mental function one with the film.

In his work "The End of St. Petersburg," he initially firmly grasps three themes. These three themes are relative and begin to struggle with the same strength, but after the inevitable development, the first two themes are linked together, and the third finally triumphs. The victor is the revolution.

Pudovkin's direction of actors' performances is incredibly appropriate and scientific. This science is difficult to define easily. Of course, this is also his greatness.

Under his own careful management, Pudovkin is often able to develop himself and express himself. This is the point of failure for other people, but for Pudovkin, it is the reason for success. However, he has only one weakness, and that is that he overbelieves in the film's composition and his own knowledge and is unwilling to trust the camera. This is the opposite of Eisenstein. However, Pudovkin's inspiration is truly rich, and all expressions and emotions often come from this inspiration.

Film Review

(1) Flower of Freedom 249

— Su Yi

Zheng Zhengqiu's film "Flower of Freedom" has been released at the Central Theater. The script is taken from the story of Yuan Shikai claiming the title of Emperor and Cai E escaping from Beijing to start an uprising in Yunnan. Zhengqiu is a drama expert who is good at singing patriotic tunes, so it seems that he has fully applied his lifelong drama style to the silver screen! He has a style that can arouse emotions in the popular, which can naturally arouse the praise of the audience. "Flower of Freedom" can be regarded as a successful work of the Star Film Company, and it is also a successful work of Zhengqiu.

In terms of light, the whole film is clear and balanced. There are one or two dim fragments, which cannot be regarded as a big flaw. In terms of pronunciation, although it is a mix of southern and northern accents, it can still be heard clearly. There are one or two places where the actors seem to be reading the script dead, looking like they are reciting textbooks, but it does not make people feel annoying. The plot of the whole film is very compact and has the effect of concentrating the audience's attention. These points can be said to be the achievements of the director, photographer, and sound engineer.

As for the actors, Hu Die can be regarded as a successful role. She plays the female detective Jin Yihong, vividly showing a smart, clever, sociable, and not-evil-hearted woman. She sets up a beauty trap to flatter General Chen Gongyue, from capturing Chen to releasing Chen. All kinds of contradictory emotions such as joy, anger, sorrow, happiness, shrew, compassion, crying, and laughing are like a tide, stirring endlessly on her face, chest, and the posture of her whole body. Hu Die is able to put in so much hard work and will be very promising in the future. Other roles, such as Zheng Xiaoqiu, who plays Lin Daping, depicts a pure and brave patriotic young soldier, who is wonderfully sincere. Sitting silently and blowing the flute, sighing and singing long songs, the heroic indignation has been stained with the essence of Zhengqiu's drama. Gong Jianong, who plays Chen Gongyue, pretends to be deaf and feigns illness and specializes in playing cunning supporting roles. However, Xia Peizhen, who plays General Chen's wife, is too rigid, which is a bit of a flaw.

In short, this kind of national film that is reasonable and affectionate is better than the recent crudely made imported films, and it is also better than the unreasonable national "Western Flowers" films. "Flower of Freedom" can be regarded as a national film worth watching.

(2) Nymph Errant (Ronny) 250

— Yan Nan

This can really be regarded as a great contribution of Ufa Company. For two hours on the New Light screen, Ponny's performance was constantly praised in the dark. Although we have always been very alienated from a large group of European stars, a good impression will never be obliterated. From the story, of course, this is an ordinary comedy, but it is an unusual film. The director's technique is very commendable. Other things such as photography are also perfect. Of course, the most exciting thing is the performance. Marc Dantzer, who plays the prince, is a pure continental-style young man. Although he is not a handsome man, he is very likable. The woman Kate De Nagy is round and jade-like, and her singing can be compared with MacDonald. None of the supporting roles are top-notch. Maybe this play is a bit trivial, because a prince who is so obsessed with the theater is too fatuous; and people who usually play with women with money, such an ending, seems unfinished. But we don't care about anything, it is transcendent in art. All the singing, dancing, and beautiful music give us unparalleled pleasure. I believe that Ufa will definitely sell well in China from this film. One more thing must be stated, it is all in French. However, its center is maintained in singing and dancing, so French will feel more novel and interesting to us, and the film has English translations (every line has it), so people who know nothing about French will not reduce the interest in watching this film.

(3) Living God of Wealth (If I Had a Million) 251

— Ai

The Living God of Wealth, which is shown simultaneously in Guanglu Lanxin, is more like seven segments pieced together than a movie. It tells the story of a rich man who, when he is critically ill, uses a novel method to distribute a huge amount of inheritance to several unfamiliar citizens. In the film, we see seven different people, each of whom gets one million US dollars out of thin air. Different results occur in different environments, and then they are divided into seven unrelated segments.

The reflection on the screen at the end can also be regarded as a segment. A poor woman in an old people's home gets a check, and she can use this huge amount of money to organize the most perfect old people's home and create a place for the general public. And she herself also becomes a close friend with that rich man. And the rich man is no longer sick. "If I had a million" certainly cannot become a reality, but the wonderful organization is worthy of being the crystallization of the collaboration of seven directors such as Paramount and Lubitsch. Small insertions and the technology of the film cannot be done by any one director, because it is too exquisite. There are more than 20 famous stars, but each person only makes a short segment, such as Jia Zuo Kebo, who only plays one of the three sailors. I can only say that everyone is very good and very responsible.

(4) "Happiness Arrives" Pack up Your Troubles 252

— Xin

This pair of stars｜Laurel and Hardy｜'s works, to say a Shanghai word, are always "bloody," and more than half of them are hard slapstick. This time, the "Happiness Arrives" in Cathay is really a timely and psychological film. Therefore, there is a lot of commotion, and everyone is going to see this "Happiness Arrives." The plot is about the two of them being forced to join the army, but unintentionally making meritorious service and being released. Then, they meddle in other people's business and look for the grandparents of a friend's child in the army, encountering all kinds of difficulties, only to meet them unintentionally. In these two unintentional good fortunes and short abilities, countless jokes are created. Originally, his achievements in the two films are almost the same, but there is no new progress.

Although slapstick films are more than half unreasonable, there are still two shallow allegories in this script. The first is the American people's hatred for joining the army, expressing the general psychology of war. The second is that many things cannot be forced, so people who are blind and blindly pursue them should be vigilant.

I think that many people think that after watching this film, they didn't laugh much. From the title of the play, they get a good omen. I think that going to laugh for two hours is not a loss for the price you paid.

Tragedy of the "Lone Army"

Settlement of the Yang Liuqing Compensation Issue 253

It is reported that Ms. Yang Liuqing, who was accidentally shot and killed while acting in the film "Lone Army," had been out of touch with her family for three years and had not returned to her hometown. After Ms. Yang's death, the Da Zhong Company found the residence of her parents in Ms. Yang's luggage and sent three telegrams urging them to come to Suzhou to take care of everything. As a result, her mother came to Suzhou. However, regarding the issue of her afterlife, Ms. Yang's mother said that this matter must be negotiated directly with her father.

Now that the film is about to be completed, the negotiation issue must be resolved first. Therefore, last week, representatives were sent to Hangzhou to handle the matter, but they did not get anything. The second negotiation was held a few days ago. As a result, a cash compensation of 3,000 was set as the minimum amount. The company was satisfied and signed a contract to settle the matter. However, it is heard that there is still a clause in the contract that stipulates that a certain percentage of the business income will be taken out as a supplementary condition, which the company also recognized. (Que Chou)

A Bill of Divorcement (Part 2) 254

— Yi

They were talking about the pending marriage issue and their going to Canada together, but Sydney felt they might not be able to go before her mother and Gray got married.

"They will hold the wedding in the New Year, right?" Kit asked hopefully.

"Probably, Kit; do you think we will still love each other in Canada! People say that places and environments are enough to change love." She said with a half-smile.

"What place, what environment can change my love for you, Pei?" Kit's eyes showed his deep love for this beautiful young lady. He put his hand into his pocket and took out a ring box. "Look, Sydney, I brought this ring for you. You will soon be the fifth-generation bride in my family to wear it."

"Kit, your mother's engagement ring!"

Sydney was numb in his arms, everything she had hoped for had now come true.

At that time, the carolers were playing music for many guests. Margaret, Gray, and Aunt Hester were all standing near their windows, admiring the beautiful singing. The lead singer suddenly said to Margaret, "Mrs. Fairfield, we would like to sing a special hymn for you and Mr. Gray."

Aunt Hester's face became stern when they associated Gray's name with Margaret, but Margaret smiled and asked them what they wanted to sing.

"If you like, Mrs. Fairfield, we will sing "God Bless the Master of this House | God Also Bless the Mistress of this House |""

Margaret was very happy, and seemed a little shy.

Their rhythmic singing aroused Aunt Hester's reaction. Unable to restrain herself and忍忍 to wait until the singing was over, she took Margaret away from the crowd.

"Margaret! How could you allow them to sing that hymn? Hilary is the master of this house, no one else, only your husband Hilary!"

The next day, Christmas morning, the table was set as usual for three people's breakfast. Aunt Hester and Margaret were sitting and eating, and Sydney walked in, cheerfully exclaiming, "Merry Christmas to you!"

Aunt Hester interjected, "Thank you for my calling card case, Sydney."

"Oh, that's a cigarette case, dear Aunt. If you give me another prayer book this year, we'll have plenty of"

She unwrapped the package placed on her left, and continued, "Hey, I expected it. Thank you very much, Aunt. Another prayer book for me!"

"Have you taught your daughter to be so rude to me, Margaret?" Aunt Hester was furious.

"Sydney!" Margaret warned her.

"Does she think I'm as easy to control as you are?"

Margaret again feigned a reprimand, "Not necessarily, dear."

"Don't you think it was she who made you suffer since you divorced your father? Isn't it she who is preventing you from marrying Gray?"
